### Q-33-DRAFTS-TAB-STATUS
Use `status=draft` — it is a STATUS param, never a scope. Fix spec 33 §3.1 to read: the Drafts tab calls `GET /motifs?scope=mine&status=draft&limit=50` (both params, explicitly). Rationale from code: (1) `scope` and `status` are two independent query params on the same route — `scope` is `^(mine|system|all)$`, `status` is `^(draft|active|archived)$`; passing `scope=draft` 422s. (2) `status` defaults to `"active"`, so a bare `GET /motifs` returns ZERO drafts — the Drafts tab MUST send `status=draft` explicitly or it renders empty forever. (3) `scope=mine` is the right companion because mined drafts are created owner-tier (`create(source="mined", status="draft")` with owner = caller); system-tier motifs are seeded active, so `scope=all` only adds rows that can never be drafts. BUILDER ACTION: (a) in the Drafts tab data hook call `motifApi.list({ scope: 'mine', status: 'draft' })` — the FE client already types `scope` and `status` as separate fields (frontend/src/features/composition/motif/api.ts:21-27), so NO client change is needed, only the correct call site; (b) ADDITIONALLY, when the Motif Studio is open in a book context, the tab must ALSO fetch `GET /motifs/book/{book_id}?status=draft` (composition-service/app/routers/motif.py:219-227, same status pattern) and merge — because mining run with `promote_target="book_shared"` (motif_mine.py:504) lands drafts in the book's SHARED tier, which `GET /motifs?scope=mine` does NOT return; skipping this makes collaborator-mined drafts invisible. (c) Test: one router test asserting `GET /motifs?scope=draft` → 422 and `GET /motifs?scope=mine&status=draft` → 200 returning the mined draft, so the spec's trap can't be re-introduced. Default I am picking (veto-able): the Drafts tab shows user-tier + book-shared drafts merged, deduped by motif id, book-shared badged.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/routers/motif.py:151-169 (scope pattern `^(mine|system|all)$` at :153 and status pattern `^(draft|active|archived)$` default "active" at :158 are SEPARATE params); services/composition-service/app/routers/motif.py:219-227 (book route carries the same status filter); services/composition-service/app/engine/motif_mine.py:444 (mined rows persist as owner-tier status='draft') and :504 (promote_target='book_shared' lands them in the book SHARED tier instead); frontend/src/features/composition/motif/api.ts:21-27 (FE client already models scope and status as distinct fields — no client change needed)

### Q-33-X12-BARE-ID
AFFIRM THE LOCK — drawer / inline-form / modal / section, no `motif-editor` panel — and stop defending it with prose. Build it this way in 3a:

(1) SHAPE (unchanged, now binding). `motif-library` is the ONLY new panel id in 3a (+ `quality-conformance` in 3c). Motif detail = a drawer INSIDE `MotifLibraryPanel`; create = inline form; adopt = `AdoptTargetModal`; the link graph = a collapsed section. Do NOT add `motif-editor`, `motif-detail`, `motif-graph`, or any `hiddenFromPalette` panel in this wave. Reason grounded in code: `frontend_tools.py:397-486` gives `ui_open_studio_panel` a single `panel_id` enum with `additionalProperties: False`, and `studioUiNav.ts:35` calls `host.openPanel(panelId)` with no params — so a panel needing `motif_id` MUST be `hiddenFromPalette` (`catalog.ts:100,279`) ⇒ dropped from `OPENABLE_STUDIO_PANELS` ⇒ out of the py enum, the contract enum, the Command Palette and the User Guide. Extracting a motif-editor panel INTRODUCES the bug.

(2) DEEP-LINK WITHOUT LEAVING THE ENUM (this is what makes the lock costless, and it is the piece 3a must actually implement). `motif-library` MUST be **bare-id openable**: `openPanel('motif-library')` with zero params renders the list (Mine tab). It MAY additionally accept an OPTIONAL `params.motifId` to pre-open the detail drawer — the host already supports this (`StudioHostProvider.tsx:52,77`, F1 seam, tested at `StudioHostProvider.test.tsx:92-127`; `studioLinks.ts:78-80` is the precedent). In-app affordances (the `NodeBadges.tsx:124` motif chip, the new scene-inspector Motifs section) call `host.openPanel('motif-library', { params: { motifId } })`; the agent calls the bare id and gets the list. This is exactly plan 30 §7 row 14's `world-map` pattern ("takes `params.mapId` but still self-resolves a default") and 38's self-resolving `world`. Panel code reads `params.motifId` defensively — `undefined` is a first-class state, never an error.

(3) MAKE IT MECHANICAL — the review trap becomes a red test, per `checklist-is-self-report-enforce-by-tests`. In `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/__tests__/panelCatalogContract.test.ts` add:
```ts
// X-12 (plan 30 §8.2): ui_open_studio_panel carries a BARE ID (frontend_tools.py:397-486).
// A hiddenFromPalette panel is therefore OUT of the agent enum, the palette and the User Guide.
// This allowlist is FROZEN. To add a row you must first extend the tool with a `params` arg
// (schema + CLOSED_SET_ARGS + contract regen + BOTH resolvers) — that is the X-12 decision, not a
// catalog edit. Deep-link an entity instead: openPanel('<hub>', { params: { <id> } }) — the F1 seam.
const HIDDEN_FROM_PALETTE_ALLOWLIST = [
  'wiki-editor','job-detail','book-reader','skill-editor','json-editor','media-version-history',
  'original-source','translation-versions','translation-review','chapter-revision-compare','welcome',
].sort();
it('hiddenFromPalette is a frozen allowlist (X-12)', () => {
  const hidden = STUDIO_PANELS.filter((p) => p.hiddenFromPalette).map((p) => p.id).sort();
  expect(hidden).toEqual(HIDDEN_FROM_PALETTE_ALLOWLIST);
});
```
(requires exporting `STUDIO_PANELS` alongside `OPENABLE_STUDIO_PANELS` from `catalog.ts` — it already is, line ~279's filter reads it.) Verified today: 68 catalog rows, 11 hidden, 57 openable — matches plan 30's baseline exactly, so the allowlist above is the true current set and the test is green on arrival. A future agent who "improves" this by extracting `motif-editor` now gets a RED test naming X-12, not a comment they can skim past.

Assert the delta + three-way equality, never a literal. If a later wave genuinely needs an entity-scoped agent-openable panel, that is the X-12 `params` extension in Wave 0 — a Frontend-Tool-Contract change, decided once, alongside X-5 — NOT a per-wave `hiddenFromPalette` opt-out.

### Q-33-PORT-TRAP-SIMPLEMODE

  const { accessToken } = useAuth();            // '@/auth' — same as BookSettingsPanel.tsx:29
  <div data-testid="studio-motif-library-panel" className="h-full">
    <MotifPanelBoundary label="motifs">

        <MotifLibraryView token={accessToken} meUserId={<user.id from useAuth()>} projectId={…} bookId={…} />
      </MotifSimpleModeProvider>

  </div>

STEP 2 — make the degrade NON-SILENT (this is the actual root cause; without it the next panel re-ships the bug).
In `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/context/MotifSimpleModeContext.tsx`:
 - add `bound: boolean` to `export type MotifSimpleMode` (line 13-17);
 - provider value (line 57) → `{ simple, setSimple, toggle, bound: true }`;
 - the out-of-provider fallback (line 66) → `{ simple: true, setSimple: () => {}, toggle: () => {}, bound: false }`, and immediately above it add `if (import.meta.env.DEV) console.error('useMotifSimpleMode() outside MotifSimpleModeProvider — Simple/Expert toggle will be inert');`.

Rationale: KEEP the optional fallback (read-only consumers like MotifCard/MatchReasonChip legitimately render provider-less in unit tests — see the comment at MotifSimpleModeContext.tsx:60-62), but NEVER render an inert control. No provider ⇒ no dead button; a provider ⇒ a live button. That is exactly `silent-success-is-a-bug`.

STEP 3 — the test that asserts the EFFECT (a rendered label changes), not the call.
New file `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/__tests__/MotifLibraryPanel.simpleMode.test.tsx`. It MUST NOT mock `../context/MotifSimpleModeContext` — the existing `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/__tests__/MotifLibraryKindToggle.test.tsx:21` does exactly that (`vi.mock(... useMotifSimpleMode: () => ({ simple: true, toggle: vi.fn() }))`), which is precisely why this trap survives the green suite. Assertions, in order:
  1. render <MotifLibraryPanel/>; expect the motif card to show the SIMPLE label text (from `kindLabelKey('sequence', true)` = 'motif.simple.kind.sequence' — its i18n defaultValue string);
  2. `await userEvent.click(screen.getByTestId('motif-simple-toggle'))`;
  3. expect that SIMPLE label text to be GONE and the EXPERT label text (`kindLabelKey('sequence', false)`) to be in the document — i.e. `expect(screen.getByTestId('motif-simple-toggle')).toHaveTextContent('Expert')` AND a card-level label assertion;
  4. `expect(toggle button).toHaveAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false')` after the click (it is `aria-pressed={simple}` at MotifLibraryView.tsx:74);
  5. one negative test: render `<MotifLibraryView token="tok" meUserId="u1" />` with NO provider → `expect(screen.queryByTestId('motif-simple-toggle')).toBeNull()` (step-2 guard proven by effect).
Wave DoD: `/review-impl` at wave close, per the run policy.

DEFAULT the PO may veto: hiding the toggle when unbound (step 2) rather than throwing. Throwing would red the existing provider-less unit mounts of MotifCard/InfoAsymmetryCard/MatchReasonChip; hiding is the non-breaking, no-dead-control choice.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/composition/motif/context/MotifSimpleModeContext.tsx:63-67 (the no-op fallback: `return { simple: true, setSimple: () => {}, toggle: () => {} }`) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/components/MotifLibraryView.tsx:38,74-76 (the only render site of the Simple/Expert toggle; `onClick={toggle}`, `aria-pressed={simple}`) · frontend/src/features/composition/components/CompositionPanel.tsx:876-889 (the ONE existing correct mount — provider wraps both motifs + conformance slots; the new studio panels must copy it) · `find -iname "*MotifLibraryPanel*"` returns NOTHING → the studio panel is unbuilt, so the trap is not yet shipped there · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/__tests__/MotifLibraryKindToggle.test.tsx:21 mocks `useMotifSimpleMode` → no existing test exercises the real toggle; `simpleMode.test.ts` only tests pure label-key fns, never a rendered label

### Q-33-BOOK-TAB-PARTITION
CLIENT-SIDE PARTITION OF ONE FETCH. Do NOT add a tier/scope query param to the backend — zero backend work. The route already emits both partition keys per row.

BUILDER INSTRUCTIONS (3a):

1) `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/api.ts` — add ONE method next to `list`/`catalog`:
   `listBook(bookId: string, params: { genre?, kind?, q?, language?, status?, limit? }, token: string): Promise<{ motifs: Motif[]; book_id: string; count: number }>`
   → `apiJson(`${BASE}/motifs/book/${bookId}${_qs(params)}`, { token })`. Envelope is `{ motifs, book_id, count }` (motif.py:241-245), NOT `{ items, total }`. `Motif` already declares `book_id?: string|null` and `book_shared?: boolean` (types.ts:43-44) — no new type needed; do NOT create a `BookMotif`.

2) `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifLibrary.ts` —
   a. Widen `LibraryScope` to `'mine' | 'book' | 'shared' | 'system' | 'catalog' | 'drafts'` (6 tabs, §3.1). Keep the existing `my` query as the `mine`/`system`/`all` feeder via `motifApi.list`.
   b. Accept `bookId: string | null` in `opts`.
   c. Add EXACTLY ONE react-query call for the book route, whose queryKey DOES NOT contain the tab:
      `useQuery({ queryKey: ['composition','motifs','book', bookId, q], queryFn: () => motifApi.listBook(bookId!, { q, limit: 100 }, token!), enabled: !!token && !!bookId && (scope === 'book' || scope === 'shared') })`
      Both tabs read that same cache entry ⇒ ONE network call, two views. Do NOT give Book and Shared separate `useQuery`s and do NOT put `scope` in the key — a reviewer who finds two `GET /motifs/book/{book_id}` fetches has found a defect.
   d. Partition in a `useMemo` (NOT in `select`, which is per-instance):
      Book tab rows = `rows.filter(r => r.book_id === bookId && !r.book_shared)` — the `book_id === bookId` test is LOAD-BEARING: the route merges the caller's globals (book_id NULL) and system rows into the same list (motif_repo.py:474-479), so without it the Mine tier is duplicated onto the Book tab.
      Shared tab rows = `rows.filter(r => r.book_shared === true)`.
   e. When `bookId` is null, hide the Book + Shared tabs entirely (the route is VIEW-grant-gated and 404s without a book — motif.py:236).

3) BUG TO FIX WHILE HERE (found reading the code, not in the spec): `_book_view` → `_redact_for_viewer` nulls `owner_user_id` for a NON-owner's shared row (motif.py:110). `useMotifLibrary`'s tier facet derives `owner_user_id == null ⇒ 'system'`, so another collaborator's shared motif would be mis-faceted as System. SUPPRESS the tier facet on the `book` and `shared` tabs (same as the catalog tab already does) and badge shared rows off `book_shared === true`, never off tier.

4) TESTS (vitest, `motif/__tests__/`): (i) with a mocked `listBook` returning [own global (book_id null), own book label (book_id=B, shared false), foreign shared (book_id=B, shared true, owner null)] — assert Book tab yields exactly the book-label row and Shared yields exactly the foreign shared row; (ii) assert `apiJson` was called ONCE for `/motifs/book/` across a `book`→`shared` tab switch (this is the anti-double-fetch regression test).

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/routers/motif.py:219-245 (GET /motifs/book/{book_id} — params are genre/kind/q/language/status/limit ONLY; no tier/scope) · motif.py:207-216 (_book_view stamps book_id + book_shared on every row) · motif.py:110 (_redact_for_viewer sets owner_user_id=None for a non-owner ⇒ the tier-facet mis-classification) · services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/motif_repo.py:474-479 (WHERE merges own-globals + system + this book's labels + this book's shared tier — the reason the book_id test is load-bearing) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/types.ts:43-44 (book_id/book_shared already on the FE Motif type) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifLibrary.ts (LibraryScope = 'my'|'catalog'|'drafts' today; no book query) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/api.ts:54+ (motifApi has no listBook)

### Q-33-CONFORMANCE-STATUS-TRAP
**Build (B) — migrate `useConformanceStatus` to react-query. REJECT (A): the spec's own recommendation is broken, and its "shipped precedent" justification is factually false.**

WHY (A) IS WRONG (amend spec 33 §7.2's option table with this): (A) claims it "mirrors how `reloadChapter`/`reloadScenes` already bridge to hand-rolled Tier-4 state." It does not. Those bridge to `useManuscriptUnit()` (`useStudioEffectReconciler.ts:25`), which is a **`createContext` PROVIDER** (`ManuscriptUnitProvider.tsx:15`) — a hoisted singleton, so the reconciler's `u.reload()` mutates the same cell the editor renders. `useConformanceStatus` has **no provider**: `SceneBrowserPanel.tsx:110` and `SceneInspectorPanel.tsx:86` each call it independently ⇒ two independent `useState` cells. A reconciler-owned instance is a **THIRD** cell no panel renders; its `refresh()` refetches into the void. (A) ships a `refreshConformance` field, a handler that calls it, green tests — and chips that stay stale. That is a false green of the repo's `silent-success-is-a-bug` class, and it ships the exact staleness X-4 exists to kill. (A) could only be made correct by ALSO hoisting the hook into a context provider — hand-rolling react-query for one query, i.e. MORE work than (B).

(B)'S COST IS OVERSTATED IN THE SPEC — it is XS, not S, and touches ZERO panel source:
- `refresh()` is DEAD API today: `grep -rn "conf.refresh\|\.refresh()" frontend/src/features/studio/panels/` returns nothing. No call site breaks.
- Both panels read ONLY `conf.dirtyChapters` (`SceneBrowserPanel.tsx:263`, `SceneInspectorPanel.tsx:110`). Preserve the `ConformanceState` return shape ⇒ **neither panel file is edited**.
- Both already sit under the app-wide `QueryClientProvider` (`App.tsx:76`; `SceneInspectorPanel` already renders `useGlossaryRoster`, a `useQuery`).
- **`EffectContext` needs NO new field** — `queryClient` is already on it (`effectRegistry.ts:14`), and every shipped handler refreshes via `invalidateQueries` (`glossaryEffects.ts:43-49`, `knowledgeEffects.ts:24-35`).

BUILDER INSTRUCTIONS (exact):

1. `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/useConformanceStatus.ts` — replace the `useState`/`useEffect`/`useCallback` body (lines 25-43) with a `useQuery`, following the studio convention at `useQualityCanon.ts:83-92`:
   - `const q = useQuery({ queryKey: CONFORMANCE_STATUS_KEY(bookId), queryFn: () => compositionApi.getConformanceStatus(bookId!, token!), enabled: !!bookId && !!token });`
   - Export the key factory from this file so handlers never guess it: `export const CONFORMANCE_STATUS_KEY = (bookId: string | null) => ['studio', 'conformance-status', bookId] as const;`
   - **Keep the exported `ConformanceState` shape byte-identical** (`status`, `dirtyChapters`, `staleChapterCount`, `loading`, `error`, `refresh`). Map: `status: q.data ?? null` · `loading: q.isLoading` · `error: q.error ? (q.error instanceof Error ? q.error.message : 'conformance unavailable') : null` · `refresh: () => { void q.refetch(); }` (keep it — it is the hook's public contract even though unused; do not silently drop it). Keep the `dirtyChapters` `useMemo` (lines 45-51) verbatim.
   - **Preserve the advisory-never-breaks-the-surface invariant** (the hook's header comment): the panels must render normally on fetch failure. `q.data` is `undefined` on error ⇒ `status: null` ⇒ `dirtyChapters` empty ⇒ chips drop. Verify no `throwOnError`/error-boundary default is set on the app's `QueryClient` (`App.tsx:76`); if one is, pass `throwOnError: false` on this query explicitly.

2. `frontend/src/features/studio/agent/handlers/motifEffects.ts` (the new Wave file) — in the `/^composition_conformance_run/` handler, add one line alongside the other invalidations, importing the key factory (never a literal): `ctx.queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: CONFORMANCE_STATUS_KEY(ctx.bookId) });`

3. Do **NOT** add `refreshConformance` to `EffectContext`. `effectRegistry.ts` is unchanged by this item.

4. TESTS:
   - `__tests__/useConformanceStatus.test.ts` — the 4 existing cases stay; wrap `renderHook` in a `QueryClientProvider` (`retry: false`, `gcTime: 0`) so the "does not fetch without a book" case still asserts `enabled:false` ⇒ `getConformanceStatus` not called. Add a 5th: a REJECTING `getConformanceStatus` yields `dirtyChapters.size === 0` and does not throw (the advisory invariant; the current suite explicitly dodged this — see its comment at the "clean status" case).
   - `agent/handlers/__tests__/motifEffects.test.ts` — assert the `composition_conformance_run` handler calls `invalidateQueries` with exactly `['studio','conformance-status',bookId]`.
   - **THE ONE THAT ACTUALLY PROVES IT** (a mocked handler test cannot — `test-injecting-a-fake-at-the-chokepoint-cannot-prove-the-chokepoint-is-wired`): an integration test rendering `SceneBrowserPanel` **and** `SceneInspectorPanel` under ONE real `QueryClient`, with the real (unmocked) `useConformanceStatus` — assert a dirty chip is present, then call `queryClient.invalidateQueries(CONFORMANCE_STATUS_KEY(bookId))` with a refetch returning a CLEAN status, and assert the chip disappears **in BOTH panels**. This is the assertion that fails under (A) and passes under (B); it is the reason for this decision and must be in the diff.

5. Panels: no source change. Re-run the existing `SceneBrowserPanel.test.tsx` / `SceneInspectorPanel.test.tsx` (they `vi.mock` the hook module, so they are unaffected) plus a live browser smoke of the two scene panels per the wave's DoD.

DEFAULT-FLAG (PO may veto): I am overriding the spec's RECOMMENDED option. If the PO prefers (A) anyway, it is only correct with an added `ConformanceStatusProvider` context hoist — which costs more than (B) and duplicates react-query. I do not recommend it.

*Evidence:* Option (A)'s premise is FALSE: `useStudioEffectReconciler.ts:25` (`const unit = useManuscriptUnit()`) resolves a **context singleton** — `frontend/src/features/studio/manuscript/unit/ManuscriptUnitProvider.tsx:15` imports `createContext`/`useContext` — which is why `reloadChapter` (`useStudioEffectReconciler.ts:57-59`) reaches the editor's rendered state. By contrast `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/useConformanceStatus.ts:22-27` is a bare `useState` loader with NO provider, instantiated independently at `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/SceneBrowserPanel.tsx:110` and `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/SceneInspectorPanel.tsx:86` ⇒ a reconciler-owned third instance's `refresh()` (`useConformanceStatus.ts:19,56`) reaches neither panel. Supporting: `refresh` has zero call sites (`grep -rn "\.refresh()" frontend/src/features/studio/panels/` → none); both panels read only `conf.dirtyChapters` (`SceneBrowserPanel.tsx:263`, `SceneInspectorPanel.tsx:110`); `EffectContext` already carries `queryClient` (`frontend/src/features/studio/agent/effectRegistry.ts:14`) and all shipped handlers refresh via it (`agent/handlers/glossaryEffects.ts:43-49`, `agent/handlers/knowledgeEffects.ts:24-35`); the react-query convention to copy is `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/useQualityCanon.ts:83-92`; app-wide provider at `frontend/src/App.tsx:76`. Spec text adjudicated: `docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/33_motif_studio.md:574-610`. No conflict with plan 30 §0 (PO-1..4 do not touch Lane-B/EffectContext).

### Q-33-GRAPH-LIST-NOT-CANVAS
LIST — confirmed by the schema, and it is now enforced, not just documented. Build `frontend/src/features/motif-studio/components/MotifGraphSection.tsx` as a collapsed section with exactly three keyboard-navigable <ul> groups (Composed of · Precedes/Preceded-by split by `direction` · Variants) fed by `GET /v1/composition/motifs/{id}/links?direction=both` (BE-M3), each row = neighbor code+name button (navigates the drawer) + Remove → `DELETE /v1/composition/motif-links/{link_id}`; add-link = inline form (kind <select> over the closed set composed_of|precedes|variant_of + a motif picker) → `POST /v1/composition/motifs/{id}/links`, with the DB trigger's 409 (motif_link_guard: self-link / cycle / cross-tier) rendered INLINE on the form carrying the trigger's own reason, never flattened into a toast. NO layout dependency may be added: no d3 / dagre / elkjs / cytoscape, and NO reuse of `reactflow` or `PlanCanvas` for motifs. Two anti-drift artifacts are part of the slice's DoD: (1) the `.callout.bad` in the 3a design draft, verbatim — "The motif graph is a LIST, not a canvas — deliberate. The data is 3 typed edge lists with no persisted positions (`motif_link` has no x/y). A force-directed view needs a layout engine + a positions migration = D-MOTIF-GRAPH-CANVAS (Wave 4/5). Do not 'fix' this with d3."; (2) a MACHINE guard — `frontend/src/features/motif-studio/components/__tests__/MotifGraphSection.test.tsx` asserts the three lists render from a mocked links payload AND reads MotifGraphSection.tsx's source to assert it imports none of /reactflow|^d3|dagre|elkjs|cytoscape/ (a prose callout is a self-report; this repo's rule is "checklist ⇒ test the effect"). Keep D-MOTIF-GRAPH-CANVAS open (gate #2, Wave 4/5) — it is what makes the call reversible. PO default they may veto: if a canvas IS wanted, it is a Wave-4/5 slice that STARTS with a `motif_link_layout(motif_id, book_id, x, y)` migration + write route — not a component swap inside 3a.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/db/migrate.py:788-796 — `CREATE TABLE motif_link (id, from_motif_id, to_motif_id, kind CHECK IN ('composed_of','precedes','variant_of'), ord, created_at)`: a pure edge table, NO x/y/position column, so there is no layout state to render on a canvas. services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/motif_repo.py:215-272 — `list_links()` returns a flat array of `{id, kind, ord, direction, neighbor:{id,code,name}}` `ORDER BY kind, ord NULLS LAST` — i.e. the API hands the FE three pre-grouped typed edge lists, exactly the list shape. Contrast: the repo's only canvas, frontend/src/features/plan-hub/components/PlanCanvas.tsx (reactflow ^11.11.4, frontend/package.json:61), works because plan nodes carry persisted positions + lane semantics; motifs carry neither, so "just reuse ReactFlow" is a migration + new write route, not a component swap. Spec grounding: docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/33_motif_studio.md:302 (the list-not-canvas rule) and :804 (D-MOTIF-GRAPH-CANVAS, gate #2).

### Q-33-X4-LANEB-MANDATORY
MUST-BUILD — confirmed by code, but the spec's sketch is WRONG in 3 places and the builder must use THIS version instead.

BUILD: new file `frontend/src/features/studio/agent/handlers/motifEffects.ts` + register it in `useStudioEffectReconciler.ts` (import next to line 21, call `registerMotifEffectHandlers()` inside the useEffect at lines 34-39). New test `frontend/src/features/studio/agent/__tests__/motifEffects.test.ts`, mirroring `knowledgeEffects.test.ts`. Delete the now-FALSE comment at `useStudioEffectReconciler.ts:9-10`.

KEY SETS — read from the hooks, not guessed (prefix-invalidate; react-query matches by array prefix):
- library family: ['composition','motifs'] (covers 'my'/'catalog'/'drafts' — useMotifLibrary.ts:74,84,95), ['composition','motif'] (useMotifDetail.ts:17), ['composition','motif-sync'] (useMotifSync.ts:15)
- candidates: ['composition','motif-candidates'] (useMotifCandidates.ts:11)
- bindings: ['composition','motif-bindings'] (useMotifBindings.ts:11) + ['composition','decompose'] (useMotifBinding.ts:25 invalidates it on every bind — mirror the PRODUCER)
- conformance: ['composition','conformance'] (useConformanceTrace.ts:15) + ['composition','arc-conformance'] (useArcConformance.ts:20)
- plan-hub chips/overlay: invalidate the ['plan-hub'] PREFIX. The overlay key is ['plan-hub','overlay',bookId] (usePlanHub.ts:39) and conformance is ['plan-hub','conformance',bookId] (usePlanHub.ts:51) — NOT ['composition',...]. Prefix-invalidating ['plan-hub'] is the established post-write precedent (usePlanNodeWrites.ts:51, usePlanMoves.ts:169).
- links: NO key exists today (no motif-link hook, no REST route — plan 30 line 246). PIN IT NOW: the wave's new link-graph hook MUST use ['composition','motif-links', motifId]; the handler prefix-invalidates ['composition','motif-links'].

PATTERN→HANDLER MAP (only DIRECT writes get a tool-name pattern):
- /^composition_motif_(create|patch|archive)/  → library family + motif-candidates
- /^composition_motif_link_/                    → motif-links (+ library family: link edits change the motif detail)
- /^composition_motif_(bind|unbind)/            → motif-bindings + decompose + conformance + ['plan-hub']

CORRECTION 1 (the one that breaks the spec's version) — `adopt`, `mine`, and `conformance_run` are PROPOSE-ONLY: `composition_motif_mine` (server.py:2993), `composition_motif_adopt` (server.py:2913+), `composition_conformance_run` (server.py:3136+) each `return {confirm_token, descriptor, title, domain, estimate}` and WRITE NOTHING. Registering a handler on those tool names fires at propose time (invalidating a cache nothing changed) and MISSES the actual write, which lands after the human confirms via the generic `confirm_action` frontend tool → POST /v1/composition/actions/confirm (ConfirmActionCard.tsx:115-129). So ALSO register a handler on the exact string 'confirm_action' that unwraps the result (reuse `unwrapToolResult` from handlers/resultEnvelope.ts), reads `descriptor`, and no-ops unless it is one of _MOTIF_ADOPT_DESCRIPTOR / _MOTIF_MINE_DESCRIPTOR / _CONFORMANCE_RUN_DESCRIPTOR (copy the literal strings from server.py) — then invalidates the same families. Scoping the confirm_action handler to those 3 descriptors is also what keeps it from double-firing with bookEffects.
  ⚠ mine + arc-import are ASYNC: confirm only ENQUEUES. Lane B at confirm-time is necessary but NOT sufficient — MotifMinePanel's poll (over BE-7c `GET /v1/composition/motif-jobs/{job_id}`) MUST itself invalidate ['composition','motifs'] on terminal status. Write that into the panel slice, not into motifEffects.ts.

CORRECTION 2 — `useConformanceStatus` (frontend/src/features/studio/panels/useConformanceStatus.ts:22-43) is hand-rolled useState/useEffect, NOT react-query, so `invalidateQueries` CANNOT reach it (repo's known `invalidatequeries-cannot-reach-hand-rolled-state` bug class). Convert it to `useQuery({ queryKey: ['composition','conformance-status', bookId], queryFn: () => getConformanceStatus(bookId, token) })`, keep the derived `dirtyChapters`/`staleChapterCount` memos and expose `refresh = refetch` so SceneBrowserPanel/SceneInspectorPanel need no change. Then the handler invalidates ['composition','conformance-status']. This conversion is IN SCOPE of this slice — without it the dirty chips stay stale and the handler is a placebo.

CORRECTION 3 — the spec's ⚠ "/^composition_generate/ is already covered by bookEffects.ts:60" is FALSE as written: bookEffects.ts:60 is `/^composition_.*(prose|draft)/`, which matches `composition_write_prose` (server.py:1217) but NOT the literal string `composition_generate` (server.py:1365). The CONCLUSION still stands — do NOT register `/^composition_generate/` — but for the real reason: composition_generate is itself propose-only (cost-gated confirm_token, server.py:1365-1380). Leave its post-confirm refresh where it is today; do not extend the new confirm_action handler beyond the 3 motif/conformance descriptors.

TESTS (Definition of Done for this slice): motifEffects.test.ts asserts, per pattern, the exact invalidateQueries key arrays above (spy on queryClient); PLUS a guard assertion that `matchEffectHandlers('composition_generate')` does NOT include the motif handler (kills the double-register regression); PLUS a test that a `confirm_action` result carrying the motif-mine descriptor DOES invalidate ['composition','motifs'] and one carrying an unrelated descriptor does NOT. Per the PO's binding policy, `/review-impl` runs at wave close and any bug it finds is fixed before the wave closes.

### Q-33-404-MINE-POLL
CONFIRMED IN CODE — and it is WORSE than the spec states: the mine job is never even created. `_enqueue_motif_job` stamps a synthetic `pid = uuid4()` for Work-less jobs (actions.py:552), but `GenerationJobsRepo.create` inserts via `INSERT INTO generation_job … SELECT $1,$2,w.book_id,… FROM composition_work WHERE w.project_id = $2` (generation_jobs.py:161-174). A random pid matches no Work ⇒ 0 rows ⇒ `has_work is None` ⇒ `raise ReferenceViolationError("project … has no composition_work row")` (generation_jobs.py:201-206). Nothing in actions.py catches it, so `POST /actions/confirm` 500s — AFTER `_claim_or_replay` consumed the token and `_precheck_or_402` reserved the billing hold (actions.py:639-644). Even if the row existed, `GET /jobs/{job_id}` gates on `_gate_work(job.project_id)` → `works.get(synthetic)` → None → 404 "work not found" (engine.py:1415-1427 + 219-227), and the MCP poll `composition_get_mine_job` is broken the same way (server.py:3207-3222 — it REQUIRES a project_id and denies on the missing Work). This is exactly the PO's CRITICAL "paid-action defect" class. It is buildable now — do NOT defer it.

BUILD IT AS BE-7c (Wave 3a prerequisite; ship before MotifMinePanel is ported). The fix is: a job's gate must derive from THAT JOB'S OWN scope, and a Work-less job must be a first-class user-scoped row — stop faking a project_id.

1. `services/composition-service/app/db/migrate.py` (generation_job DDL block, ~line 265): add idempotent `ALTER TABLE generation_job ALTER COLUMN project_id DROP NOT NULL;` + `ALTER COLUMN book_id DROP NOT NULL;` + `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_generation_job_owner ON generation_job(created_by, created_at DESC);`. (No FK on project_id, so no constraint churn.)
2. `app/db/models.py:364-365`: `project_id: UUID | None = None`, `book_id: UUID | None = None`.
3. `app/db/repositories/generation_jobs.py` `create()`: accept `project_id: UUID | None` + a new `book_id: UUID | None = None` kwarg. When `project_id is None`, use a plain `INSERT … VALUES` (NO `SELECT FROM composition_work`) writing `created_by`, NULL project_id and the passed book_id, still calling `emit_job_event` inside the same tx. Leave the existing INSERT…SELECT + ReferenceViolationError branch untouched for project-scoped creates.
4. `app/routers/actions.py:534-562` `_enqueue_motif_job`: DELETE `pid = project_id if project_id is not None else uuid4()`. Pass `project_id` through (may be None) and add `book_id=` — for `mine_motifs`, `payload["book_id"]` when `scope=='book'` else None; for `analyze_reference`, None; `conformance_run` keeps its real project_id. `enqueue_job(..., project_id=str(pid) if pid else "")` (the redis XADD field must be a str; worker/job_consumer.py:372-382 shows mine/import read only `job.created_by` + `job.input`, so project_id is vestigial for them).
5. `app/routers/engine.py:1415-1427` `get_job`: replace the unconditional `_gate_work` with a scope-derived gate — `if job.project_id is not None:` → existing `_gate_work(..., GrantLevel.VIEW)`; `elif job.book_id is not None:` → `authorize_book(grant, job.book_id, user_id, GrantLevel.VIEW)` (OwnershipError→404, InsufficientGrant→403); `else:` → `if job.created_by != user_id: raise HTTPException(404, "job not found")`.
6. `app/mcp/server.py:3193-3222` `composition_get_mine_job`: make `project_id: str | None = None` and apply the SAME 3-way gate; keep the cross-Work IDOR check (`job.project_id != pid`) only when a project_id was passed. Update ALL THREE schema sources (decorator description + Annotated types + the frontend/tool contract entry) — FastMCP strips undeclared ones.
7. `app/routers/internal_job_control.py:165,182` (Retry re-drive — `mine_motifs` is `is_worker_drivable` ⇒ retryable=True): pass `job.project_id` (may be None) + `book_id=job.book_id` to `create`, and `project_id=str(job.project_id) if job.project_id else ""` to `enqueue_job`.
8. FRONTEND: no change — `motifApi.mineConfirm` already polls `compositionApi.getJob` → `GET /v1/composition/jobs/{id}` (frontend/src/features/composition/motif/api.ts).

TESTS (the whole bug survived because these were mocked away):
- `tests/unit/test_motif_mine.py`: call the REAL `_enqueue_motif_job` (do NOT monkeypatch it — that is what tests/unit/test_conformance_run_worker.py:201 does and it is why this shipped) with project_id=None → assert the row persists; then `GET /v1/composition/jobs/{id}` = 200 for `created_by`, 404 for another user; book-scoped mine (book_id set, no Work) = 200 for a book-VIEW grantee, 403 for a non-grantee.
- Integration (real PG, `pytest.mark.xdist_group("pg")`): `GenerationJobsRepo.create(None, book_id=None, …)` inserts (today it raises ReferenceViolationError).
- `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/__tests__/MotifMine.test.tsx`: mock at the FETCH level (GET /v1/composition/jobs/{id} → pending → completed) so the poll loop actually runs, not the poll function.
- LIVE SMOKE (mandatory — paid action): run a corpus mine on the test account with a local lm_studio model, poll the real route to `completed`.

Note for the PO (veto-able default): I chose nullable project_id/book_id on the existing `generation_job` over a separate user-scoped job table because it keeps ONE job home, ONE worker dispatch, ONE poll route and ONE FE call; the code comment at actions.py:548-551 already admits the synthetic-pid hack this removes.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/routers/actions.py:552 (`pid = project_id if project_id is not None else uuid4()`) → services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/generation_jobs.py:161-174 (INSERT…SELECT FROM composition_work) + :201-206 (raise ReferenceViolationError "project … has no composition_work row") ⇒ mine/import jobs are never inserted; and services/composition-service/app/routers/engine.py:1415-1427 → :219-227 (`_gate_work` → `works.get(project_id)` is None → HTTP 404 "work not found") ⇒ every Work-less job poll 404s. MCP twin: services/composition-service/app/mcp/server.py:3207-3222. Vestigial project_id proven at services/composition-service/app/worker/job_consumer.py:372-382 (mine/import use only `job.created_by` + `job.input`). Mocked-away test: services/composition-service/tests/unit/test_conformance_run_worker.py:201 monkeypatches `_enqueue_motif_job`.

### Q-33-MINE-NO-CANCEL
CONFIRM THE SPEC: no Cancel button in the mine "paid action in flight" state. The code proves the worker is not cancellable AND that faking it would corrupt the job row.

BUILDER INSTRUCTION (3a, MotifMinePanel):
1. In-flight state (`mine.confirm.isPending` — after confirm, while polling BE-7c's `GET /v1/composition/motif-jobs/{job_id}`): render progress ONLY — a spinner/status line + the job status text from the poll envelope. Render NO Cancel button, NO Stop button, and NOT a disabled Cancel button either (a disabled cancel is still a fake affordance — the concern's point).
2. Render an explicit honesty line beside the progress, i18n key `motif.mine.noCancel`, defaultValue: "Mining can't be stopped once it starts — you're only charged for the run you confirmed." Do not hide the absence of cancel; state it.
3. DO NOT touch `useMotifMine.cancel()` (hooks/useMotifMine.ts:44) — it is the PRE-confirm cancel (`setEstimate(null)`, dismisses CostConfirmCard before any spend) and is wired at MotifMinePanel.tsx:45 as CostConfirmCard's `onCancel`. It stays exactly as-is. Do not rename it, do not repurpose it into a job cancel. The free cancel lives BEFORE confirm; there is none after.
4. TEST (add to frontend/src/features/composition/motif/__tests__/MotifMine.test.tsx): with the mine job in flight (confirm mutation pending / poll returning status 'running'), assert `queryAllByRole('button', { name: /cancel|stop/i })` is EMPTY, and assert the `motif.mine.noCancel` copy is present. This test is what keeps a later contributor from "helpfully" adding a Stop button.

WHY (not taste — mechanics): (a) job_consumer.py:372-377 calls run_mine_motifs with NO cancel_check while every sibling op threads it, and motif_mine.py has zero `cancel` refs → the mine loop cannot abort; (b) generation_jobs.py:588-600 `update_status` is an unguarded `UPDATE … WHERE id=$1`, so a CAS-cancel (internal_job_control.py:214-224) gets OVERWRITTEN back to 'completed' by the finishing worker at job_consumer.py:280 → the user would see "cancelled" and still get billed + get the drafts; (c) the cancel route is /internal S2S, not gateway-exposed, and motif/api.ts has no job-cancel call — zero FE reach today.

DEFAULT THE PO CAN VETO: I am NOT ordering real cancellation in this wave. Making mine truly cancellable is a separate, structural change (thread cancel_check through run_mine_motifs' per-candidate LLM loop + add a terminal-status guard to the SHARED update_status, which every op uses + expose a gateway cancel route), and it still would not refund the LLM calls already made. If the PO wants a real cancel, it is a follow-up row, not a 3a slice. NOTE FOR THE DEFER REGISTER (origin 3a, gate 2 large/structural, target: post-Wave-3 backlog): D-MOTIF-MINE-REAL-CANCEL — mine worker ignores cancel_check and update_status has no terminal guard, so a P3 cancel is silently clobbered; if a mine cancel is ever exposed, the guard must land FIRST or it ships a fake-cancel.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/worker/job_consumer.py:372-377 (mine_motifs dispatched to run_mine_motifs with NO cancel_check, unlike :302/:308/:319/:364); services/composition-service/app/engine/motif_mine.py (grep 'cancel' → 0 hits); services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/generation_jobs.py:588-600 (update_status = unconditional UPDATE … WHERE id=$1, no terminal guard → worker's 'completed' at job_consumer.py:280 clobbers a CAS 'cancelled'); services/composition-service/app/routers/internal_job_control.py:186-224 (cancel exists but is internal-token S2S, not gateway-exposed); frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifMine.ts:44 + components/MotifMinePanel.tsx:45 (existing cancel() is the PRE-confirm CostConfirmCard dismiss — keep)

### Q-33-ARC-TEMPLATE-DRIFT-SCOPE
CONFIRM the spec's answer — Wave 4 (`arc-templates`, spec 34 M4). The code proves the two scopes are different QUESTIONS with different comparands, so they are two panels, not one panel with three radio buttons.

THE CODE FACT (services/composition-service/app/routers/conformance.py, one handler, three branches):
- `scope=arc` (:376-389) → `_resolve_book_arc(structure_repo, arc_id, book_id)` then `compute_arc_report(..., arc=node, by_structure=True)` — the durable SPEC arc (a `structure_node`) vs the realized `motif_application` bindings keyed by `structure_node_id`. Comparand = PROSE. It PERSISTS a snapshot (`_persist_conformance_best_effort`).
- `scope=arc_template_drift` (:390-404) → same node, but then `node.arc_template_id` provenance → `arc_repo.get_visible(user_id, node.arc_template_id)` → `compute_arc_report(..., arc=<the arc_template row>, by_structure=False)`. Comparand = the TEMPLATE. Different entity class, different report keying (annotation-keyed, not structure-keyed), and it deliberately NEVER persists (see the comment at :385-387). It also has a failure mode `scope=arc` does not have: **422 `NO_TEMPLATE_PROVENANCE`** when the arc was authored from conversation (`node.arc_template_id IS NULL`).

BUILDER INSTRUCTIONS — Wave 3c (`quality-conformance`, the 5th card in `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/QualityHubPanel.tsx:13-18` `CARDS`):
1. The panel's scope state and its API signature are a CLOSED SET OF TWO. In the panel's api module type it literally as `scope: 'chapter' | 'arc'` — do NOT type it `string` and do NOT add `'arc_template_drift'`. TypeScript then compile-blocks the third scope; that is the enforcement, per the Frontend-Tool-Contract "closed-set arg ⇒ enum" rule.
2. Render the exclusion as a visible `.callout.bad` in the panel body, i18n'd (studio namespace), verbatim intent: "This panel answers *did the prose realize my plan* (spec vs prose). *How far has my arc drifted from the template it came from* is a different question — it lives in the **Arc Templates** panel." Do not make it a deep-link/button in 3c (the panel does not exist yet in Wave 3); plain text.
3. Add a guard test in the panel's vitest file: render the panel, assert the scope control exposes exactly the two options and that no request the panel can issue contains `scope=arc_template_drift` (e.g. assert on the fetch spy's URL across every scope the toggle can reach). This is the "checklist ⇒ test the effect" rule — the callout alone is a self-report.
4. Do not "fix" it by pointing the panel at `arc_template_drift` — that would silently answer a different question.

WAVE 4 (spec 34 M4, `arc-templates` panel) owns the drift surface, and it is BE-NONE: the route ships. It must render all three states — report, 422 NO_TEMPLATE_PROVENANCE ("this arc was authored directly; it has no template to drift from"), 404 NOT_FOUND (template deleted/foreign). MCP-side parity (`composition_arc_template_drift`, still a `_pending_engine` stub at mcp/server.py:4673-4700) stays parked as BE-8/M5 and must delegate to `compute_arc_report(..., by_structure=False)` — never a second engine.

Rationale: `arc-templates` is not registered in the panel catalog until Wave 4, and a link to an unregistered `panel_id` is exactly the silent-no-op bug class. ### Q-33-X6-RESOURCE-REF
X-6 does NOT gate either consumer. Build 3b + 3a/3c now on the two ALREADY-SHIPPED focus seams; X-6 gates only the "an AGENT points at this object" leg (a wire/JSON ref in an MCP payload), which neither consumer here is — both are in-process React onClicks inside the same StudioHost tree. This matches spec 32's already-ratified ruling for the sibling panel (32_arc_inspector.md:405-415: "X-6 gates the 'agent points at this arc' leg only... Decompose, don't block") and contradicts no §0 sealed decision. Note the default for the PO to veto: I am treating spec 33's own "blocking: false" as correct and NOT holding the motif wave for the AN-12 section.

THE RULE TO WRITE DOWN (this is the whole answer): the focus seam is chosen by the RECEIVING panel's existing target-resolution mechanism. Pick wrong => silent no-op (the exact no-silent-no-op bug class the panel_id enum was added to kill). Two seams exist, both shipped:
  (A) BUS-driven panels — scene-inspector resolves its target from useStudioBusSelector(s => s.activeSceneId) (useSceneInspector.ts:25). It NEVER reads props.params. => openPanel('scene-inspector', {params:{sceneId}}) IS A SILENT NO-OP. Must host.publish({type:'scene', sceneId, chapterId}) THEN host.openPanel('scene-inspector', {focus:true}).
  (B) PARAMS-driven panels — quality-canon/quality-promises read props.params (QualityCanonPanel.tsx:33); producer is openPanel(id, {focus:true, params:{bookId, focusRuleId, ...}}) (PlanHubPanel.tsx:65-78). openPanel calls updateParameters when the panel is already open (StudioHostProvider.tsx ~L85), so re-links land on an open panel.

TRAP 1 (ordering) — the 'chapter' bus event RESETS activeSceneId (host/types.ts:96). Focus the chapter FIRST, publish the scene SECOND. Canonical shipped example: StudioFrame.tsx:110-116 (resolveJump).
TRAP 2 (null chapterId) — SCENE nodes carry chapterId: null; only CHAPTER nodes carry it (usePlanHub.ts:117 maps n.chapter_id; PlanHubPanel.tsx:50 states it). The 'scene' bus event REQUIRES a chapterId (it also sets activeChapterId, which drives the editor via ManuscriptUnitProvider.tsx:321-325), so a scene's chapterId must be walked from its PARENT chapter node via parent_id (available: plan-hub/types.ts:64; usePlanHub.ts:156 already walks it).

CONCRETE BUILD INSTRUCTION:
1. usePlanHub.ts:117-119 — add `parentId: n.parent_id` to NodeContent (one additive line; arcs get parentId: null at :111).
2. plan-hub/types.ts:116 — widen PlanOverlayRef.kind to 'canon' | 'thread' | 'motif'. REQUIRED COMMENT: motif refs are synthesized CLIENT-SIDE from the chip the node already carries; the /plan-overlay endpoint never sends kind:'motif'. (Reuse this one vocabulary + the one existing callback — do NOT add a second onOpenMotif seam; that would break one-name-for-one-concept/DA-10.)

When onOpenRef is undefined keep the plain <span> — never a dead button (the H4.1 fallback rule CanonBadge already follows, NodeBadges.tsx:1-5). Keep the existing data-testid `plan-badge-motif-${nodeId}-${motif_id}` unchanged.

Resolve the chapter id: c = view.nodeContent[nodeId]; chapterId = c.kind === 'chapter' ? c.chapterId : view.nodeContent[c.parentId ?? '']?.chapterId ?? null. Then: if c.kind === 'scene' && chapterId => host.focusManuscriptUnit(chapterId); host.publish({type:'scene', sceneId: nodeId, chapterId}); host.openPanel('scene-inspector', {focus:true}). If neither (arc rollup) => return, no-op with no panel churn.

Motif ref on a CHAPTER node calls view.select(nodeId) and does NOT open scene-inspector.

### Q-33-OCC-412-SERIALIZE
SERIALIZE + CONFLICT STRIP — but the spec's premise is HALF WRONG, and the builder must not implement it as written. Only 3a is OCC. 3b cannot self-412 (no If-Match, no version column) and must be serialized for a DIFFERENT reason. Build exactly this:

(1) NEW `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifWriteChain.ts` — port the PROVEN single-flight chain from `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/useSceneInspector.ts:40-104` verbatim in shape (it is the fix that already shipped for this exact bug class):
```ts
export function useMotifWriteChain(motif: Motif | null, token: string | null, onUpdated: (m: Motif) => void) {
  const motifRef = useRef<Motif | null>(motif);            // LIVE mirror — version is read from HERE, never a closure
  useEffect(() => { motifRef.current = motif; }, [motif]);
  const chainRef = useRef<Promise<void>>(Promise.resolve());
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const [conflict, setConflict] = useState(false);
  const patch = useCallback((args: MotifPatchArgs): Promise<void> => {
    const targetId = motifRef.current?.id ?? null;         // capture the entity AT CALL TIME
    const run = async () => {
      const cur = motifRef.current;
      if (!token || !cur || cur.id !== targetId) return;   // selection moved → DROP the queued edit
      setSaving(true);
      try {
        const updated = await motifApi.patch(cur.id, args, cur.version, token);  // version from the MIRROR (prior link bumped it)
        motifRef.current = updated; onUpdated(updated);
      } catch (e) {
        if ((e as {status?:number}).status === 412) {      // AFTER serialization a 412 IS a genuine external change
          setConflict(true);
          const fresh = await motifApi.get(targetId!, token); motifRef.current = fresh; onUpdated(fresh);
        } else { /* setError */ }
      } finally { setSaving(false); }
    };
    const next = chainRef.current.then(run, run); chainRef.current = next; return next;
  }, [token]);
  return { patch, saving, conflict, dismissConflict: () => setConflict(false) };
}
```
(2) 3a — EVERY instant-commit control over a motif (Drafts-tab Promote = `motifApi.promote` → the same If-Match PATCH at `api.ts:186`; Discard/archive; any status/kind/tension chip or select on `MotifCard`/`MotifFacetRail` that writes) calls `chain.patch(...)`, NEVER `motifApi.patch` directly, and carries `disabled={saving}` (belt-and-braces so the serialization is visible, not just correct).
(3) 3a form — `useMotifEditor` routes its Save mutation through the SAME chain instance (so Save + a chip can't collide) and KEEPS its two existing correct behaviours: the id-only re-seed guard (`useMotifEditor.ts:73-83` — a refetch must not clobber in-progress edits) and `conflict` state. Fix the missing half: today `onError` at `useMotifEditor.ts:126-129` sets `conflict` and NEVER re-fetches — the chain's 412 branch supplies the re-fetch. Render `MotifStateBoundary` (`components/MotifStateBoundary.tsx:22`) as the conflict strip ("This motif changed elsewhere — reload to see the new version"); the form keeps the user's values for copy-out.
(4) 3b — DO NOT wire If-Match here. `useMotifBinding.ts:31/39/49/56` (`swap`/`rebindRole`/`clearMotif`/`chainIt`) hit `PATCH|DELETE /works/{pid}/outline/{node}/motif[/role][/chain]` (`plan.py:855/946/1009/1061`), which take NO `If-Match` (no `_parse_if_match` anywhere in `plan.py`; OCC exists only on `/motifs/{id}` — `motif.py:89`), and they write `motif_application`, which has NO version column (spec §8.3). A 412 there is IMPOSSIBLE. The real race is the replace semantics: every writer does `delete_for_nodes` then insert (`plan.py:843-844`, `motif_select.py:470`), so a role-rebind racing a swap applies a role to a row the swap already deleted (silently lost), and two swaps land in nondeterministic order. So: hoist ONE `chainRef` into `useMotifBinding` and funnel all four mutationFns through it (separate react-query mutations do NOT serialize against each other), plus `disabled={isPending}` on the chips. State the reason in the code comment as replace-semantics ordering, not 412 — a comment blaming 412 sends the next reader hunting a header that doesn't exist.
(5) TESTS (mirror the proven one at `frontend/src/features/studio/panels/__tests__/useSceneInspector.test.ts:77`): `useMotifWriteChain.test.ts` — (a) two rapid chip writes fired WITHOUT awaiting (deferred-resolve mock of `motifApi.patch`) both land and the 2nd call's `expectedVersion === 2` (reds on the un-chained code); (b) a real 412 sets `conflict`, re-fetches, and does NOT clear the form; (c) selection moves before the queued link runs ⇒ the queued edit is DROPPED (not applied to the new motif). `useMotifBinding.test.ts` — swap+rebindRole fired back-to-back issue in order (the 2nd request starts only after the 1st resolves).
Spec amendment to fold into 33 §3.0/§8.3: "self-412s" applies to 3a only; 3b serializes for write-ordering over a versionless replace-table.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/studio/panels/useSceneInspector.ts:40-104 (the shipped single-flight chain: live `nodeRef` mirror + `chainRef.current.then(run, run)` + capture-target-at-call-time + 412⇒refetch) · test frontend/src/features/studio/panels/__tests__/useSceneInspector.test.ts:77 · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/api.ts:67-74 (`patch` sends `If-Match`) and :186 (`promote` = an instant-commit PATCH) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifEditor.ts:126-129 (412 sets `conflict` but never re-fetches — the gap) and :73-83 (id-only re-seed, keep) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifBinding.ts:31,39,49,56 (four unserialized react-query mutations, NO If-Match) · services/composition-service/app/routers/plan.py:855,946,1009,1061 (motif/role/chain routes — no `If-Match` header param; `_parse_if_match` appears only in motif.py:89, arc.py:79, canon.py:61) · services/composition-service/app/db/migrate.py:882 (`motif_application` non-unique node index, no version column)

### Q-33-UNDO-TOKEN-SCOPE
CONFIRMED BY CODE — token-undo is CHAPTER-scope only. Build 3b's binding lens with a kind-gated Undo:

(1) SCENE node (scene-inspector Motifs section): affordances are Bind/Change (PATCH /v1/composition/works/{pid}/outline/{nid}/motif {motif_id}) and Clear (PATCH same URL with {motif_id: null}, or DELETE). NEVER render an Undo button and never send `undo_token` on a scene — `_bind_scene_motif` (plan.py:801-852) returns none, and the MCP tools composition_motif_bind/unbind reject a scene node outright (motif_select.py:463 `target.kind != "chapter"` -> MotifSwapError -> uniform 404). The scene's inverse is a RE-BIND: before issuing the scene PATCH, capture the node's prior `motif_id` from the already-shipped GET /works/{pid}/outline/motif-bindings?chapter_id=… (frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:181-185) into local state, and label the affordance "Revert to <prior motif>" (or "Clear" when there was no prior binding) — implemented as a second PATCH with the prior motif_id (or {motif_id: null}). Do not call it "Undo" and do not present it as an exact inverse: a scene re-bind is a fresh ledger row (annotations.bound_via='manual_scene'), not a restore.

(2) CHAPTER node (PlanDrawer chapter variant): the swap response carries `undo_token` (plan.py:942). Keep it in component state (session-only, never persisted) and render Undo, which PATCHes the SAME URL with body {undo_token} (plan.py:881-886 -> undo_motif_swap -> {undone: true, ...}), then invalidates the ['composition','decompose',projectId] query.

(3) FIX-NOW while you are in this file — chapter CLEAR must go through PATCH {motif_id: null}, NOT DELETE. `useMotifBinding.clearMotif` (frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifBinding.ts:49-53) uses DELETE today, and the chapter DELETE handler (plan.py:989-993) returns `{chapter_node_id, archived_scene_ids, cleared}` with NO undo_token — so a chapter clear as currently wired is silently un-undoable even though the engine supports it. Switch clearMotif to PATCH {motif_id: null} (which runs apply_motif_swap with new_motif=None and DOES return undo_token, plan.py:936-943) so Undo works for clear too; keep DELETE only for the scene path.

(4) ONE render guard, not two: `const canUndo = node.kind === 'chapter' && !!lastUndoToken` — derived from the response actually received, so a missing token can never produce a live-but-dead button.

(5) Tests (3b DoD, literal): FE vitest in frontend/src/features/composition/motif/__tests__/ — (a) render the Motifs section on a scene node after a successful bind -> `expect(screen.queryByRole('button', {name: /undo/i})).toBeNull()`; (b) render the chapter variant, resolve the PATCH mock with `{undo_token: {...}}` -> Undo appears; click -> assert fetch called with method PATCH and a body containing `undo_token`; (c) chapter mock that resolves WITHOUT undo_token -> no Undo button. Backend: services/composition-service/tests/unit/test_scene_motif_bind.py already asserts the scene path's shape — add one assertion that `'undo_token' not in out` for the scene bind response, so the contract is machine-pinned on both sides.

Default I am taking (veto-able): the scene affordance is labelled "Revert to <prior motif>" / "Clear", NOT "Undo" — one word for one concept, so "Undo" always means the token round-trip.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/routers/plan.py:845-852 (scene bind response — no undo_token) vs plan.py:936-943 (chapter swap — returns undo_token) and plan.py:881-886 (the only undo_token consumer); services/composition-service/app/engine/motif_select.py:463 (`target.kind != "chapter"` -> MotifSwapError, so MCP composition_motif_bind/unbind at app/mcp/server.py:2748,2825 are chapter-only); plan.py:989-993 (chapter DELETE clear returns NO undo_token) vs frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifBinding.ts:49-53 (clearMotif uses DELETE today); `grep -rn "undo_token|undoToken" frontend/src` -> 0 hits (zero FE consumers confirmed).

### Q-33-REGEN-UNGATED
SHIP REGENERATE UNGATED. The Regenerate button calls the SAME REST route through the SAME existing FE client the shipped ComposePanel uses — `compositionApi.generateUrl(projectId)` (frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:389) for the SSE path, or `generateAuto()` (api.ts:398) for the auto path. Builder instruction, concretely:

1. DO NOT add a confirm dialog, cost estimate, spend warning, `/actions` propose→confirm round-trip, or any other pre-spend interstitial to the Regenerate button. Wire it as a plain click → existing generate call, identical to ComposePanel's Generate. Inventing a confirmation convention on this one button is a spec-28 AN-8 defect ("a reviewer finding a new confirmation convention here has found a defect") and is REJECTED.
2. Reuse the existing hook (`frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useCompositionStream.ts`) rather than adding a second generate caller. One name, one concept.
3. Pass the author's steering text through the field the route already accepts for exactly this (engine.py:208 — "regenerate → the author's steering text. Stored, never on the wire").
4. If /review-impl flags "Regenerate spends tokens with no gate" during this wave's DoD, the correct response is to point at defer row D-COMPOSE-GENERATE-UNGATED — NOT to bolt a gate on. Closing that finding by gating Regenerate alone is a defect, not a fix.

WHY (this is the part the spec gets slightly wrong, and the builder should know): the spec says the MCP twin "IS Tier-W confirm-gated" while REST is not, implying the MCP path has a spend guardrail REST lacks. It does not. `_execute_generate` (actions.py:388) is reached through a confirm TOKEN, but it never calls `_precheck_or_402` (actions.py:517) — only motif_mine (:642), analyze_reference (:692) and conformance_run (:722) do. So NEITHER generate path has a spend precheck; the only delta is the confirm token. The gap is narrower than stated, which is further reason not to fork a bespoke gate onto one FE button to close it.

DEFER ROW SCOPE CORRECTION (carry this into the row): the eventual fix is NOT "port the MCP gate to REST." It is ONE route-level precheck inside engine.py:326 (+ the chapter twin at engine.py:899), calling the already-existing `_precheck_or_402` / `get_billing_client()` seam. Because both ComposePanel and Regenerate — and the MCP `_execute_generate` path, which calls the engine router coroutine in-process — funnel through that route, a single gate there fixes every call site at once. That is precisely why gating the FE button is the wrong layer.

NOT A CRITICAL BLOCKER under the PO's stop-and-ask policy: ungated generate is a real defect but it is not the "paid-action defect that charges the user for nothing" class (the motif-mine poll 404). Generate delivers the draft it spends on. Build proceeds; the row stays open.

DEFAULT NOTED FOR PO VETO: this ships a user-visible token spend on a single click with no estimate. That is the status quo the shipped ComposePanel already has, so Regenerate introduces no NEW exposure — but if the PO wants a spend gate before this wave ships, the correct instruction is "action D-COMPOSE-GENERATE-UNGATED now, at engine.py:326," not "gate the button."

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/routers/engine.py:326 — `@router.post("/works/{project_id}/generate")`; its Depends list (lines 329-350: works/outline/structures/scene_links/canon/jobs/book/glossary/knowledge/llm/... /grant) contains NO billing client and no confirm token → ungated, confirmed. Contrast services/composition-service/app/routers/actions.py:331-340 (`_GENERATE_DESCRIPTOR` → `_execute_generate`, confirm-token gated) — but note actions.py:388 `_execute_generate` itself never calls `_precheck_or_402` (actions.py:517), which only motif_mine (actions.py:642), analyze_reference (actions.py:692) and conformance_run (actions.py:722) invoke → neither generate path has a spend guardrail. services/composition-service/app/clients/billing_client.py:4 names the defect in its own docstring: "the cowrite ENGINE spends LLM tokens with zero pre-spend check — `_execute_generate`". FE path Regenerate must reuse: frontend/src/features/composition/api.ts:389 (`generateUrl`) / :398 (`generateAuto`), driven by frontend/src/features/composition/hooks/useCompositionStream.ts.

### Q-33-BOOKSHARED-QUOTA
THE ADOPTER'S QUOTA — verified against the code, and the defer row's premise is refuted (there is no ledger involved; usage-billing never sees an adopt). Close D-MOTIF-BOOKSHARED-QUOTA with NO runtime change.

WHY (three code facts):
(a) The "quota" is NOT a billing ledger — it is a local row-count ceiling: `_adopt_quota_guard` (services/composition-service/app/routers/motif.py:134-146) calls `MotifRepo.count_adopted_by_owner` = `SELECT count(*) FROM motif WHERE owner_user_id=$1 AND source='adopted' AND status<>'archived'` (motif_repo.py:914-922), against `settings.motif_max_adopt` (app/config.py:161, DEFAULT 0 = unlimited — so it does not even bite in default config).
(b) The adopt INSERT stamps `owner_user_id` = the caller for EVERY target including `book_shared` (motif_repo.py `adopt`/`_adopt_once`, INSERT column list ~:102-111; `book_shared` only changes the idempotency key + the advisory lock, never the owner stamp). So the counter's predicate (`owner_user_id = caller`) and the write's stamp are the SAME predicate — the adopter's-quota answer is true by construction, not by luck.
(c) usage-billing is not on this path at all: `_execute_motif_adopt` (app/routers/actions.py:564) contains NO `_precheck_or_402` call — those exist only at actions.py:642 (`motif_mine`), :692, :722, i.e. the LLM-spending effects. Adopt spends nothing. `grep -i motif services/usage-billing-service/**/*.go` → zero hits. There is no "usage-billing owner" to consult; gate #4 was mis-applied.
Policy check: adopter's-quota is also the CORRECT policy — if a book_shared adopt charged the book owner, an EDIT-grantee could exhaust the owner's ceiling across a grant boundary (a cross-tenant resource-exhaustion vector). Charging the caller is the safe default.

BUILDER INSTRUCTION (mechanical, ~30 min):
1. NO change to motif.py / motif_repo.py / actions.py.
2. BUILD INSTRUCTION (3c, `quality-conformance` panel):

     <div data-testid="conformance-advisory-banner" role="status" className="rounded border border-amber-300 bg-amber-50 px-2 py-1 text-[11px] text-amber-800 dark:border-amber-700 dark:bg-amber-950/30 dark:text-amber-300">
       {t('motif.conf.advisoryBanner', { defaultValue: 'Advisory — unverified. This signal is coarse and gates nothing.' })}

   )}
   Note the predicate is `!== true`, not `=== false`: a missing/undefined field must FAIL HONEST (show the banner). Never let the FE derive or default the flag to calibrated.

NOT a new user setting / env flag: `motif_conformance_calibrated` is an existing deploy-time honesty gate wired to a calibration harness (config.py:164-169), not a per-user knob — leave it exactly where it is. The GUI's only job is to echo it.

### Q-33-GRAPH-409-TRIGGER
BUILD IT AS SPEC'D — inline on the form, 409, relaying a CLASSIFIED reason (NOT the raw pg message). Concrete contract:

**BE — `services/composition-service/app/routers/motif.py`, in the new BE-M3 `POST /motifs/{motif_id}/links`:**
1. **Pre-check self-link in the app, before the INSERT:** `if body.to_motif_id == motif_id: raise HTTPException(409, detail={"code":"MOTIF_LINK_GUARD","reason":"self_link"})`. This is REQUIRED, not belt-and-braces: for `precedes`/`composed_of` the trigger's cycle CTE seeds `walk` at `NEW.to_motif_id`, so a self-link satisfies `EXISTS(node = NEW.from_motif_id)` and is raised as **`motif_link cycle`** (migrate.py:843-852) — only a `variant_of` self-link ever reaches the table CHECK `motif_link_distinct` (migrate.py:795). Without the pre-check the "self" reason is non-deterministic by kind.
2. Wrap `MotifRepo.create_link` (motif_repo.py:275):
   - `except LookupError` → **404** `{"code":"NOT_FOUND"}` (H13 — no existence oracle).
   - `except asyncpg.UniqueViolationError` → **409** `{"code":"MOTIF_LINK_EXISTS","reason":"duplicate"}` (the `UNIQUE(from,to,kind)` at migrate.py:796 — a duplicate edge is NOT the trigger; give it its own reason).
   - `except asyncpg.CheckViolationError as exc` → **409** `{"code":"MOTIF_LINK_GUARD","reason": _classify(exc), "kind": body.kind}` where `_classify` returns `"self_link"` if `getattr(exc,"constraint_name",None)=="motif_link_distinct"`, else `"cycle"` if `"cycle" in str(exc)`, else `"cross_tier"` if `"cross-tier" in str(exc)`, else `"invalid"`. (Both trigger RAISEs carry `ERRCODE='check_violation'` — migrate.py:836, 850 — so `CheckViolationError` catches all three classes.)
3. **NEVER put `str(exc)` in the response body.** Do NOT copy the `outline.py:574` / `plan.py:743` pattern (`400 {"code":"CONSTRAINT","detail": str(exc)}`) here — it is both the wrong status (spec + plan row BE-M3 say 409) and a **tenancy leak**: the cross-tier RAISE interpolates BOTH endpoints' `owner_user_id` and `book_id` into the message (migrate.py:834-835), so relaying it verbatim ships another user's UUIDs to the caller. "Relay the trigger's reason" = relay the classified `reason` enum, not the pgerror text.

**FE:**
- `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/api.ts` — add `listLinks/createLink/deleteLink` + export `type MotifLinkGuard = 'self_link'|'cycle'|'cross_tier'|'duplicate'|'invalid'` and `motifLinkGuardReason(err)`: returns the reason iff `err.status === 409` and `err.body.detail.code` is `MOTIF_LINK_GUARD`/`MOTIF_LINK_EXISTS`, else `null`. This works today with no api-layer change: `apiJson` already attaches `status` + the parsed `body` to the thrown Error (frontend/src/api.ts:159-163), and FastAPI nests the dict under `detail`.
- NEW `hooks/useMotifLinks.ts` — owns list/create/delete and a `formError: MotifLinkGuard | null`. On submit failure: `const r = motifLinkGuardReason(e); if (r) setFormError(r) else <toast>`. **A guard reason NEVER reaches the toast layer**; the form values are preserved (no reset) and the submit stays enabled.
- NEW `components/MotifGraphSection.tsx` (drawer section + library-foot section; list, not canvas) renders `formError` inline under the kind/neighbour pickers in a `role="alert"` `aria-live="polite"` block.
- Copy (motif i18n namespace): `self_link` **and** `cycle` share ONE string — the spec's sentence verbatim: *"A motif cannot precede itself, and a cycle would make the succession chain unresolvable."* `cross_tier` → *"Links must stay within one tier — a private motif cannot link to a shared or system motif."* `duplicate` → *"That link already exists."* **(Default I picked, veto-able: self+cycle share one message because the spec's own sentence covers both; and the duplicate-edge 409 renders inline too, rather than as a toast, for consistency.)**

**Tests (Definition of Done):**
- BE `tests/.../test_motif_links_router.py`: (a) A→A `precedes` → 409 `reason=self_link`; (b) A→B then B→A `precedes` → 409 `reason=cycle`; (c) private → `book_shared` → 409 `reason=cross_tier`; (d) same edge twice → 409 `reason=duplicate`; (e) **leak assertion** — `"owner=" not in json.dumps(resp.json())` and no endpoint owner UUID appears in the body.
- FE vitest on `MotifGraphSection`: mock `apiJson` to reject with `{status:409, body:{detail:{code:'MOTIF_LINK_GUARD', reason:'cycle'}}}` → assert the inline `role="alert"` copy is in the DOM AND the toast spy was NOT called.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/db/migrate.py:788-863 — motif_link DDL + guard: :795 `CONSTRAINT motif_link_distinct CHECK (from_motif_id <> to_motif_id)` (self-link, only reachable for variant_of); :796 `UNIQUE(from,to,kind)` (duplicate = UniqueViolation, not the trigger); :833-837 cross-tier `RAISE EXCEPTION 'motif_link cross-tier: from(owner=%,shared=%,book=%) to(...)' USING ERRCODE='check_violation'` (← interpolates both owners' UUIDs: relaying str(exc) is a tenancy leak); :843-852 cycle `RAISE EXCEPTION 'motif_link cycle on % via %' USING ERRCODE='check_violation'` (its CTE seeds at NEW.to_motif_id ⇒ a precedes/composed_of self-link is reported as a CYCLE). services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/motif_repo.py:275-320 create_link — docstring already states it raises LookupError / UniqueViolationError / CheckViolationError. frontend/src/api.ts:159-163 — apiJson throws `Object.assign(new Error(...), {status, code, body})`, so the FE can discriminate 409 + code with no api-layer change. Anti-pattern to NOT copy: services/composition-service/app/routers/outline.py:574 and app/routers/plan.py:743 (`400 {"code":"CONSTRAINT","detail": str(exc)}`). Spec: docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/33_motif_studio.md:305 + plan 30 row BE-M3 (33_motif_studio.md:442) — "409 from the motif_link_guard trigger — relay the trigger's reason, do not flatten it to 500".

### Q-33-STALE-PIN-REPIN
BUILD Re-pin in 3b — as a dedicated ledger-only endpoint, NOT by re-calling the swap URL. Do not defer: the write is 90% built already.

THE DRIFT IS REAL AND UNACTIONABLE TODAY: plan_overlay.py:108-123 (_MOTIF_CHIPS_SQL) ships pinned_version (ma.motif_version) + live_version (m.version); nodePresentation.ts:242 computes stale = live_version > pinned_version; NodeBadges.tsx:124-145 renders amber + ↑ on a non-interactive <span> with no onClick. Nothing anywhere can bump the pin.

⚠ THE TRAP (why the obvious fix is WRONG): PATCH /works/{pid}/outline/{node}/motif with the SAME motif_id does re-pin to live (_bind_scene_motif, plan.py:801-852, writes "motif_version": motif.version at plan.py:835 then delete+insert at plan.py:843-844) — but (a) it re-runs bind_motif() role resolution (motif_select.py:197), silently CLOBBERING any hand-rebound role written via PATCH …/motif/role → set_role_binding (motif_application.py:137-163), and (b) on a CHAPTER node that same URL runs apply_motif_swap — archives scenes, regenerates prose (plan.py:867-880) — while chips DO render on chapter/arc nodes (node_ref = COALESCE(outline_node_id, structure_node_id), plan_overlay.py:112). A blind re-bind would destroy a chapter's scenes on a "Re-pin" click. Build the endpoint below instead.

SLICE R1 — BE repo (services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/motif_application.py, beside set_role_binding at :137): add
  async def repin(self, project_id, node_id, *, motif_version: int, role_bindings: dict, annotations: dict, conn) -> int
running ONE UPDATE motif_application SET motif_version=$3, role_bindings=$4::jsonb, annotations=$5::jsonb WHERE project_id=$1 AND outline_node_id=$2, returning rowcount (same parse as set_role_binding). No INSERT — stays compatible with BE-M1's partial UNIQUE index (one row per outline_node_id).

SLICE R2 — BE route (services/composition-service/app/routers/plan.py, register beside rebind_node_motif_role at :1010 and chain_node_motif at :1062): POST /works/{project_id}/outline/{node_id}/motif/repin, empty body. Steps in order:
 1. work = await _require_work(works, grant, user_id, project_id) (EDIT, same as the role route).
 2. node = await outline.get_node(node_id); 404 {"code":"NOT_FOUND"} if None or node.project_id != project_id (H13 uniform — mirror plan.py:1030-1033).
 3. app = first of await apps.by_nodes(project_id, [node_id]); 404 if none or app.motif_id is None.
 4. motif = await MotifRepo(get_pool()).get_visible(user_id, app.motif_id); 404 if None (deleted/foreign motif).
 5. if motif.version == app.motif_version → 200 {"node_id", "repinned": false, "pinned_version": app.motif_version} — idempotent no-op, NO write.
 6. ROLE MERGE (the whole point — never clobber the author's cast work): compute the live version's declared roles via bind_motif(SelectedMotif(motif=motif, score=1.0, match_reason={}), cast_index, throwaway ChapterPlan) exactly as _bind_scene_motif does (plan.py:826-834). Then merged = for each role key the LIVE version declares: KEEP app.role_bindings[k] if present, else take the fresh auto-resolved value; DROP role keys the new version no longer declares. annotations = {**(app.annotations or {}), "repinned_from": app.motif_version}.
 7. await apps.repin(...) in one Tx; return {"node_id", "motif_id", "repinned": true, "pinned_version": motif.version, "previous_version": app.motif_version, "unresolved_roles": [k for k,v in merged.items() if v is None]}.
This touches ONLY the ledger row — no scene archive, no prose regen — so it is safe on scene AND chapter nodes. Free action (zero LLM spend) ⇒ no propose/confirm gate.

SLICE R3 — BE binding-lens payload (plan.py:1100-1131, _assemble_motif_bindings): the 3b lens cannot even SHOW the drift today — it emits motif_id/motif_name/motif_source/role_bindings/match_reason/beat_key and NO version. motif_by_id already holds the live motif (plan.py:1195-1199), so add to each BoundMotif: "pinned_version": app.motif_version, "live_version": motif.version, "stale": (motif.version or 0) > (app.motif_version or 0). Reuse the chip contract's exact field names (nodePresentation.ts:23-24) — one name for one concept.

SLICE R4 — FE (frontend/src/features/composition/motif/): add pinned_version/live_version/stale to the BoundMotif type in types.ts (beside motif_version at :182); add a `repin` useMutation to useMotifBinding.ts (beside rebindRole at :39) → apiJson(`${BASE}/works/${projectId}/outline/${nodeId}/motif/repin`, {method:'POST', token}), onSuccess: invalidatePreview + invalidate the plan-overlay query so the amber hub chip clears; export it from the hook's return (currently { swap, rebindRole, clearMotif, chainIt, regenerateScene, commitAndGenerate }). In 3b's Motifs section / MotifBindingCard: when binding.stale, render an amber row `pin v{pinned_version} → v{live_version}` plus a `Re-pin` button (data-testid="motif-repin") calling repin.mutate(), disabled while pending, toast on error.

SLICE R5 — NodeBadges stays READ-ONLY (my default; PO may veto). Do NOT turn the hub chip into a button — the badge row is a dense read-only summary and it is where DOCK-2 fork risk lives. Just make the stale chip's existing title= point at the action: `${title} · pin v{p} → v{l} (stale) — Re-pin in the scene inspector` (NodeBadges.tsx:130-133). The ACTION lives only in 3b's binding lens.

TESTS (each must red on old code):
 • pytest services/composition-service/tests: (1) repin bumps motif_version to live; (2) a role hand-set via set_role_binding SURVIVES a repin (the clobber regression — the one that matters); (3) a role key removed in the new version is dropped and a newly-added role is auto-resolved; (4) repin on an already-fresh pin returns repinned:false and writes nothing; (5) 404 on unbound node / foreign node / deleted motif; (6) repin on a CHAPTER node leaves its outline_node rows unarchived (proves it never fell into apply_motif_swap).
