### Q-33-SUGGEST-REPLACES-FLAT-LIST
REPLACE — but SCOPED to the binding surface, with the flat list kept as a "Browse all" tab. Six concrete instructions:

(1) SCOPE THE REPLACE. `useMotifCandidates` has TWO consumers: `ChapterMotifBindings.tsx:36` (per-scene bind — an outline node exists) and `ArcTimelineEditor.tsx:21` (arc-template timeline cells — NO outline node exists, so BE-M4's node-scoped suggest CANNOT serve it). Replace only in the ChapterMotifBindings path. ArcTimelineEditor/ArcTimelineGrid/ArcTimelineMobileList keep the flat list, unchanged.

(2) SwapMotifPopover props: keep `candidates` (the flat browse-all list) and ADD `suggested?: RankedCandidate[]` + `suggestState: 'idle'|'loading'|'error'|'ready'`. When `suggested === undefined` render EXACTLY today's flat list with NO tab strip (the arc-timeline call sites are then byte-for-byte unchanged and their existing tests stay green). When `suggested` is provided, render a 2-tab popover: **Suggested** (default; name + score + reason) and **Browse all** (the existing flat list). On suggest error or `suggested.length === 0`, default to the Browse-all tab with an inline "Couldn't rank — showing all motifs" note — never render the empty-popover "No other matches" string (`SwapMotifPopover.tsx:33-34`), which would lie.

(3) NEW hook `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifSuggest.ts` → BE-M4, `enabled: open && !!nodeId`. FETCH LAZILY ON POPOVER OPEN, never on mount: BE-M4 runs `embed_query` (`motif_retrieve.py:222`), a provider embedding round-trip per request; eager-fetching per scene row would fire N embeddings on render of an N-scene chapter. `SceneMotifBindingRow` (`ChapterMotifBindings.tsx:83`) owns the hook and feeds `suggested`; `useMotifCandidates` stays as the browse-all source; the existing `candidatesByNode` prop (`ChapterMotifBindings.tsx:23,61`) remains the caller-supplied override.

(4) BE-M4's query param is `node_id`, NOT `chapter_id` (spec 33:443 says `?chapter_id=` — wrong). The bind surface is per SCENE node (`ChapterMotifBindings.tsx:56` passes `s.id`), and the MCP handler already takes a generic `node_id` (`server.py:2244`) + validates `node.project_id == pid`. Accept any outline-node kind. Route: `GET /v1/composition/works/{project_id}/motifs/suggest?node_id=&limit=10&detail=summary|full`.

(5) DO NOT copy the MCP handler's arg wiring verbatim (spec 33:443's "reuse the MCP handler's body") — it is BUGGY, and the bug is the whole reason this question feels marginal. `server.py:2251` passes `beat_role=None, tension=getattr(node, "tension_target", None)`, but `OutlineNode` (`models.py:142-176`) has NO `tension_target` field — it has `tension` (0..100) and `beat_role`. So tension is always None (`_tension_band` returns a constant 0.5, `motif_retrieve.py:121-124`) and `_build_query_text(None, None)` returns "" → no query vector → `retrieve()` takes the DEGRADE branch on EVERY call (`motif_retrieve.py:218-228, 249-252`), returning `cosine: 0.0, degraded: true`, genre-only ranking. Fix BOTH call sites (the new REST route AND `server.py:2249-2252`) to pass `beat_role=node.beat_role, tension=node.tension`. Otherwise the Suggest button ships a genre sort wearing a "ranked + explained" label — the repo's own silent-success-is-a-bug class.

(6) DO NOT feed the retriever's `match_reason` into the shipped `MatchReasonChip` — it would CRASH. FE `MatchReason` (`types.ts:100-106`) is `{tension:number, genre:string[], precond:string, cosine:number, summary:string}`; the retriever returns `{tension,genre,precond,cosine}` all FLOAT (+ optional `degraded`). `MatchReasonChip.tsx:30` calls `reason.genre.join(', ')` → TypeError on a number. Add `SuggestMatchReason = {tension:number; genre:number; precond:number; cosine:number; degraded?:boolean}` and a `SuggestReasonChip` (or a discriminated branch inside MatchReasonChip); surface `degraded: true` as a "ranked without semantic match" caption.

TESTS (all in wave 3b's DoD): SwapMotifPopover.test.tsx — (a) `suggested` given ⇒ Suggested tab is default and shows score+reason; (b) tab switch ⇒ flat list; (c) `suggested` undefined ⇒ no tab strip (arc-timeline parity); (d) suggest error ⇒ Browse-all tab + notice. useMotifSuggest.test.tsx — no fetch while the popover is closed; fetch on open. BE test_motif_suggest_rest.py — 200 with ranked candidates + match_reason; uniform 404 on a node from another Work; asserts `retrieve` was called with `tension=node.tension` and `beat_role=node.beat_role`; asserts `degraded` is ABSENT when the node has a beat_role and the embed is stubbed.

DEFAULT I AM PICKING (veto-able): the Suggested tab is the DEFAULT tab when suggest succeeds. Rationale — the flat 100-row list is unranked and unexplained; the whole point of GG-1 is that the human gets the same ranked answer the agent gets, deterministically and for $0.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifCandidates.ts:13 (flat `motifApi.list({scope:'all',limit:100})`) · ChapterMotifBindings.tsx:23,36,61 (the `candidatesByNode[s.id] ?? candidateOpts` per-node-override-with-flat-fallback seam already exists) · ArcTimelineEditor.tsx:21 (2nd consumer, NO outline node ⇒ replace cannot be global) · services/composition-service/app/mcp/server.py:2244-2252 (`beat_role=None, tension=getattr(node,"tension_target",None)`) vs services/composition-service/app/db/models.py:142-176 (OutlineNode has `tension`/`beat_role`, NO `tension_target`) ⇒ services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/motif_retrieve.py:218-228,249-252 (empty qtext ⇒ qvec None ⇒ degrade branch, cosine 0.0, degraded=true on every row) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/types.ts:100-106 + MatchReasonChip.tsx:30 (`reason.genre.join(', ')` — string[] vs the retriever's float ⇒ runtime TypeError)

  under `"quality"`: `"conformanceTitle"`, `"conformanceDesc"` (exactly mirrors the existing `promisesTitle`/`promisesDesc`/`canonTitle`/`canonDesc` hub-card pair).

  `python scripts/i18n_translate.py --ns studio`
  DO NOT pass `--force`. `plan_namespace` (i18n_translate.py:339-364) carries every existing valid translation (present + non-empty + placeholder-faithful + not in `_FAILED.json`) and re-translates ONLY the missing/broken keys. So this run costs 5 new keys × 17 langs, not 722 × 17, and structurally cannot clobber existing text. `--force` would re-translate all 722 keys per language — wrong tool, real risk. Backend: LM Studio on :1234 with `google/gemma-4-26b-a4b-qat` (i18n_translate.py:52-53); it must be running.

  (b) no `frontend/src/i18n/locales/*/_FAILED.json` file exists. `_FAILED.json` is the script's no-silent-drop report: a key that survived 3 heal rounds is left as the ENGLISH source and listed there. If one appears, re-run `python scripts/i18n_translate.py --ns studio --langs <code>` (a namespace listed in `_FAILED.json` is force-retried key-level, see :419) until it clears.

Add `frontend/src/i18n/__tests__/studioParity.test.ts` as a copy of `campaignsParity.test.ts` but importing en + ALL 17 locale `studio.json` (campaigns only guards 3 locales — do not repeat that under-coverage). Assert per locale: identical flattened key set · every `{{placeholder}}` preserved · no empty value. Verified safe to add: all 17 are at exact parity at HEAD, so it is green on arrival and REDS the instant someone adds an en key without regenerating — which is the enforcement this question was really asking for ("checklist ⇒ test the effect").

### Q-33-DONT-TOUCH-LIST
GG-8's don't-touch list STANDS AS WRITTEN, and it is code-true — a reviewer who finds any of the six files in the wave-33 diff (other than the single carve-out below) has found a defect. Builder instruction:

1) NEVER edit for a new panel: `StudioDock.tsx`, `StudioFrame.tsx`, `UserGuidePanel.tsx` — all three consume `catalog.ts` exports (`STUDIO_PANEL_COMPONENTS` / `OPENABLE_STUDIO_PANELS`) and pick up `motif-library` + `quality-conformance` automatically the moment their `STUDIO_PANELS` rows land (GG-8 step 2). Adding a row to `catalog.ts` IS the registration.

2) NEVER edit: `studioUiNav.ts` / `useStudioUiToolExecutor.ts`. `studioUiNav.ts:32-35` reads `args.panel_id` and passes the raw string to `host.openPanel(panelId)` — it contains no panel-id literals. The panel_id enum lives ONLY at `services/chat-service/app/services/frontend_tools.py:400-402` (GG-8 step 6) + the regenerated `contracts/frontend-tools.contract.json` (step 7). If you feel the urge to add an id on the FE side, you are editing the wrong file.

3) NEVER edit `tools.controller.ts` — and here is the positive proof, not just a prohibition: all four tools this wave drives from the FE are ALREADY in `FE_BRIDGE_TOOL_ALLOWLIST` (api-gateway-bff `tools.controller.ts:24-30`): `composition_conformance_run` (:25), `composition_motif_mine` (:26), `composition_motif_adopt` (:27), `composition_get_mine_job` (:29). There is nothing to add. If you find yourself wanting to add `composition_motif_link_create` / `_delete` / `_bind` / `_unbind`, STOP — those are WRITES, and the controller's own contract at `:21-22` says "NOTHING here writes or deletes". Writes go over the BE-M3 REST routes (spec 33 §4, line 442), never the bridge. That urge IS the wrong turn the spec warns about.

4) THE ONE SANCTIONED CARVE-OUT (authorized here, so it is NOT a wrong turn and NOT a review finding): `CATEGORY_ORDER` at `useStudioCommands.ts:20-22` is the only list inside a don't-touch file that is hand-maintained rather than derived from `catalog.ts`. It is ALREADY missing `'quality'`, even though `catalog.ts:81-91` declares the category and `catalog.ts:266-270` ships five panels using it — so `CATEGORY_ORDER.indexOf('quality')` returns -1 and every quality panel sorts ABOVE `editor` in the command palette. `quality-conformance` makes it six. RULE: if a wave introduces a panel whose `category` is absent from `CATEGORY_ORDER`, that array MUST be extended — it is the sole legitimate reason to touch `useStudioCommands.ts`. For wave 33 specifically, apply the one-line fix: insert `'quality'` after `'storyBible'` in `CATEGORY_ORDER` (useStudioCommands.ts:21). Cover it by asserting in `src/features/studio/palette/__tests__/useStudioCommands.test.ts` that every distinct `category` on `STUDIO_PANELS` appears in `CATEGORY_ORDER` (a set-containment assertion, not a literal list) — that turns this whole class of drift into a machine guard so no future wave has to re-adjudicate it. Both `'storyBible'` and `'quality'` then exist, so no OTHER edit to that file is permitted.

### Q-33-LLM-SMOKE-MODEL-REF
DECIDE: **explicit `model_ref` (a `user_model_id` UUID) + `model_source: "user_model"` on every paid path — never a "default model for capability X" resolve, and never a platform env fallback for the smoke.** Two of the three paths already carry it; ONE (regenerate) carries nothing and must be BUILT to require it.

**(a) mine — already end-to-end; nothing to build, only to smoke.** `MotifMinePanel` mounts `ModelRolePicker capability="chat"` (MotifMinePanel.tsx:9,23) → `useMotifMine.mint.mutationFn(modelRef)` (useMotifMine.ts:23) → `motifApi.minePropose` sends `model_ref` + `model_source: 'user_model'` (api.ts:148-149) → MCP propose → `/actions/confirm` → `_execute_motif_mine` puts `payload["model_ref"]` into the job spec (actions.py:657) → `mine_motifs` reads `input["model_ref"] or settings.motif_deconstruct_model_ref` (motif_mine.py:522) and **fails closed with ValueError on empty** (motif_mine.py:339-342). ⚠ **HARD RULE FOR THE SMOKE: leave `MOTIF_DECONSTRUCT_MODEL_REF` empty (its default, config.py:201). Do NOT set it to make the smoke pass.** A platform fallback would green the smoke even if the picker's UUID never reached the engine — i.e. it would hide precisely the bug this DoD row exists to catch. The smoke's job is to prove the FE-selected UUID travelled FE → MCP → confirm → job spec → provider-registry.

**(b) conformance-run — carries model_ref, but under the WRONG KEY (M-BUG-4). Fix, then smoke `scope='arc'` only.** The MCP tool already hard-requires it for arc scope (server.py:3149-3151: `"model_ref is required when scope='arc'"`), and `_ConformanceRunArgs` is `ForbidExtra` with `arc_id` (server.py:3105-3117) while `motifApi.arcConformanceRunPropose` sends `arc_template_id` (api.ts:257) → 422 before the model_ref ever matters. Fix M-BUG-4 (send `arc_id` = a **structure_node.id**), then smoke with `{project_id, scope:'arc', arc_id:<structure_node uuid>, model_ref:<lm_studio uuid>, model_source:'user_model'}`. **Do NOT smoke chapter scope** — the worker terminates it with a ValueError by design (motif_conformance_run.py:75-80: `scope='arc'` only; chapter is the synchronous GET trace).

**(c) regenerate-to-beat — the real bite. The route does not exist AND the FE sends NO body: `motifApi.regenerateToBeat` (api.ts:300-304) POSTs with no model at all.** When you write `POST /v1/composition/works/{project_id}/scenes/{node_id}/regenerate-to-beat`, make `model_source` + `model_ref` **REQUIRED body fields → 400 `action_error` when absent**, mirroring `_execute_generate` (actions.py:414-419, which 400s on a missing `model_ref` and then `UUID(model_ref)`s it into `engine_router.GenerateBody`). **Explicitly forbid any "resolve the user's default chat model" fallback** — `user_default_models` is EMPTY for the test account, so that path resolves nothing and yields a silent no-op/500 on a PAID action (the exact class of defect the PO named CRITICAL). FE: thread a required `modelRef` prop from `ConformanceTraceView` (a `ModelRolePicker capability="chat"`, same as MotifMinePanel) → `useMotifBinding.ts:66` → `api.ts:301` body `{model_ref, model_source:'user_model'}`; disable the Regenerate button while `modelRef == null`. Add a unit test asserting `POST …/regenerate-to-beat` with no `model_ref` → 400 (fail-closed), so the default-model trap cannot regress in.

**THE SMOKE RECIPE (paste into wave 3a and 3c DoD as a literal step):**
1. Resolve the ref live (lm_studio must be up; $0): `SELECT user_model_id, alias, capability_flags FROM user_models WHERE owner_user_id='019d5e3c-7cc5-7e6a-8b27-1344e148bf7c' AND is_active;` → pick a chat-capable **lm_studio** model (e.g. Qwen2.5 7B Instruct). Never hardcode the UUID in code or a test — it is smoke input only.
2. Drive it **through the live browser** (Playwright, built FE, not raw stream — a raw-stream smoke cannot prove the FE picker wired the UUID): select that model in the panel's ModelPicker → Mine (propose → confirm → poll to `completed`) ; Conformance-run (arc) → poll to `completed` ; Regenerate → 2xx + a new draft revision.
3. VERIFY evidence string (literal token): `live smoke: motif mine + conformance_run(scope=arc) + regenerate-to-beat, GUI-selected lm_studio model_ref <uuid>, model_source=user_model, jobs terminal completed ($0 local)`. Paste the poll payloads; a claim without pasted output does not satisfy the DoD.

**Default the PO can veto:** no new setting/env is introduced for this (SET-1..8 — the model is a per-user BYOK choice, already surfaced by the existing ModelPicker); the smoke intentionally runs with the platform fallback empty.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/mcp/server.py:3149-3151 (`model_ref is required when scope='arc'`) · services/composition-service/app/engine/motif_mine.py:339-342 + :522 (fails closed on empty model_ref; `input["model_ref"] or settings.motif_deconstruct_model_ref`) · services/composition-service/app/config.py:201 (`motif_deconstruct_model_ref: str = ""` — the platform fallback is EMPTY by default) · services/composition-service/app/routers/actions.py:414-419 (generate 400s when `model_ref` is absent — the pattern regenerate-to-beat must copy) · services/composition-service/app/routers/actions.py:657 + :733 (payload `model_ref` rides into the mine / conformance_run job spec) · services/composition-service/app/engine/motif_conformance_run.py:75-80 (worker supports `scope='arc'` ONLY) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/api.ts:148-149 (mine already sends `model_ref` + `model_source:'user_model'`) · api.ts:257 (conformance-run sends the wrong key `arc_template_id` — M-BUG-4) · api.ts:300-304 (`regenerateToBeat` POSTs **no body** — no model at all) · frontend/src/features/composition/motif/components/MotifMinePanel.tsx:9,23 (`ModelRolePicker` → explicit user_model_id)

### Q-33-TOURS-OPTIONAL
SKIP. `motif-library` does NOT join any role tour in v1. GG-8 step 10 for spec 33 becomes: **"tours.ts / tourCatalog.ts — NO CHANGE. Do NOT add a `tourAnchor` to the `motif-library` row in `catalog.ts` (step 2 row is exactly `{ id: 'motif-library', component: MotifLibraryPanel, titleKey, descKey, category: 'storyBible', guideBodyKey }` — six fields, no seventh). Do NOT touch `frontend/src/features/studio/onboarding/tours.ts`, `tourCatalog.ts`, or `__tests__/tours.test.ts`."** Builder does nothing for step 10 and marks it N/A in the wave DoD.

WHY the code settles it (three independent reasons):
1. **There IS no "author" tour to join.** `STUDIO_TOURS` (tours.ts:46-119) has exactly 6 ids: `core`, `writer`, `worldbuilder`, `translator`, `enricher`, `manager` (+ the editor/composer deep-dive tours, all of which are `panelId: 'editor'` / `'compose'`-only and machine-asserted to be so at tours.test.ts:61-68 / 87-94). The spec's phrase "the author tour" names nothing in the codebase, and neither surviving candidate fits: `writer` = compose→editor→grammar→heatmap→planner (drafting loop); `worldbuilder` = glossary→wiki→knowledge (canon/lore). A motif library is craft-level and belongs to neither sequence.
2. **The role-tour sequences are LOCKED by a machine guard, not free-form.** `tours.test.ts:16-27` hardcodes `ROLE_STEPS` and asserts `expect(steps.map(s => s.panelId)).toEqual(panelIds)` — exact array equality. Joining a tour is therefore not "optional polish": it forces edits to `catalog.ts` (add `tourAnchor`), `tours.ts` (a `roleStep(...)`), `tours.test.ts` (the frozen sequence), and `intro.tour.<role>.motifLibrary.{title,body}` × 18 locales via `scripts/i18n_translate.py`. That is a real, non-trivial cost for a step nobody asked for.
3. **Its two sibling specs already made this exact call the same way.** `32_arc_inspector.md` §6 step 9: "tours.ts — **skip** — not a role-tour step in v1." `34_arc_templates_and_deconstruct.md` §6 step 9: "*(skip)* — not a role-tour step in v1." Batch-wide consistency: NO new panel in waves 1-8 joins a role tour. Deciding otherwise for `motif-library` alone would make it the only Wave-1..8 panel in a tour, for no stated reason.

Discoverability is NOT harmed by skipping — that is what the other GG-8 steps buy: the panel auto-appears in the Command Palette and the User Guide from its `catalog.ts` row (`guideBodyKey` is mandatory, X-3), and the agent can open it via the `panel_id` enum + description gloss (step 6). The tour is one of four discovery paths, and the weakest.

DEFAULT-NOTE for the PO (veto-able): if you later want motif discovery in onboarding, the cheap follow-up is a **`storyBible` deep-dive tour** (a new `tourCatalog` entry alongside the editor/composer deep-dives) covering glossary→wiki→motif-library→arc-templates — NOT a step bolted into the frozen `writer`/`worldbuilder` sequences. That is a separate, post-batch #19-Wave-5 item, not this build.

*Evidence:* frontend/src/features/studio/onboarding/tours.ts:46-119 (STUDIO_TOURS — the 6 tour ids; no 'author' tour exists; `roleStep()` at :33-44 throws at module-init if a referenced panel has no catalog `tourAnchor`) · frontend/src/features/studio/onboarding/__tests__/tours.test.ts:16-27 (`ROLE_STEPS` + `expect(steps.map(s=>s.panelId)).toEqual(panelIds)` — the role sequences are frozen by an exact-equality guard) · frontend/src/features/studio/panels/catalog.ts:110,114-266 (`tourAnchor?: string` is optional and present on ONLY the 12 role-tour panels; `glossary` :128 and `wiki` :139 are the storyBible ones) · docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/32_arc_inspector.md §6 step 9 and 34_arc_templates_and_deconstruct.md §6 step 9 (both: "skip — not a role-tour step in v1") · docs/specs/2026-07-01-writing-studio/33_motif_studio.md:527+ §6 step 10 (the open item being closed)

If a concurrent Track C entry has appeared in one of the three since you started, re-read the file, keep your additions additive alongside theirs, re-run step (3)+(4) — do not resolve it by overwriting the JSON.

RULE 3 — staging in the shared checkout (this is the "never git add -A" clause made executable): immediately before each commit, `git add <explicit path> <explicit path>` → verify with `git diff --cached --name-only` that ONLY your files are staged (drop any foreign pre-staged file with `git restore --staged <path>`) → then `git commit -m "..."` with NO pathspec. Do NOT use `git commit -- <path>`: that form commits the WORKING TREE, not the index, and would silently sweep a concurrent agent's in-flight edits to that same shared file into your commit.

Default I am choosing (veto-able): Wave 3 proceeds on schedule with no handoff document and no wait on any other track.

### Q-33-ARCHIVED-SOFT
CONFIRMED — soft archive, exactly as the spec states, and the whole backend already exists. Do NOT add a schema/migration, do NOT add a status column to `motif_application`, do NOT add a hard-delete route.

WHAT IS ALREADY TRUE (no build needed):
- Archive = `DELETE /motifs/{id}[?book_id=]` → `MotifRepo.archive` / `archive_shared` = `UPDATE motif SET status='archived'` (owner-only, or a SHARED book-tier row EDIT-gated). Nothing else is touched, so the `motif_application` ledger row survives by construction — that table has no status column at all (migrate.py:869-884), and the `motif_id` FK is only `ON DELETE SET NULL`, which never fires because archive is an UPDATE.
- Restore = `PATCH /motifs/{id}` with `{ status: 'active' }` + `If-Match: <version>` (OCC). `MotifPatchArgs.status` already exists (db/models.py:832) and the FE already uses this exact call for draft-promote (`api.ts:186`).
- List already filters by status: `status: str = Query(default="active", pattern="^(draft|active|archived)$")` (routers/motif.py:158, :226).

BUILD (wave 3a), file-by-file:
1. `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifLibrary.ts` — add `const [showArchived, setShowArchived] = useState(false)` and an `archivedQuery` that MIRRORS the existing `draftsQuery` block (lines 93-100): params `{ scope: 'all', status: 'archived', q, limit: 100 }`, queryKey `['composition','motifs','archived', q]`, `enabled: !!token && scope === 'my' && showArchived`. In the `motifs` useMemo (line ~104) concat `archivedQuery.data ?? []` AFTER `query.data` (so archived rows sort last) before the facet filter. Export `{ showArchived, setShowArchived }`. Two queries — NOT a widened `status=all` — because the router's status is a single exact enum value and widening it would have to be re-landed in the REST route, the MCP tool schema and the contract JSON (the 3-schema-sources trap). The toggle applies to the `my` scope only (catalog is server-side active-only; drafts has its own status).
2. `frontend/src/features/composition/motif/components/MotifFacetRail.tsx` — add a `Show archived` checkbox (`data-testid="motif-show-archived"`) bound to `setShowArchived`, rendered only when scope==='my'.
3. Motif card — when `m.status === 'archived'`: apply `.strike` to the name AND render a literal "Archived" chip (glyph + word + hue, never hue alone — §3.0 a11y rule); Edit/Archive actions are ABSENT (not disabled), replaced by a single `Restore` action calling `motifApi.patch(id, { status: 'active' }, m.version, token)` then invalidating the `useMotifLibrary` key (read the key from the hook, don't guess) per spec §584.
4. FIX A REAL GAP FOUND WHILE ADJUDICATING (fix-now, one line each): `motifApi.archive(motifId, token)` (api.ts:75-77) and `motifApi.patch(...)` (api.ts:67-74) both DROP `book_id`, but both routes accept `?book_id=` for the SHARED book-tier path. As written, a grantee archiving/restoring a book-shared motif gets `{archived:true}` / a 404 while the owner-keyed repo touched nothing — a silent-success no-op (the exact "silent success is a bug" class). Add an optional `bookId?: string` arg to both, append `?book_id=` when present, and pass it from the card whenever the row is `book_shared`.
5. Panel root carries `data-testid="studio-motif-library-panel"` (the `studio-<id>-panel` convention).

TESTS (each is a literal DoD item):
- `MotifLibraryArchived.test.tsx` (new, mirrors MotifLibraryKindToggle.test.tsx): toggle OFF ⇒ only the active list call fires and no archived row renders; toggle ON ⇒ the `status='archived'` call fires, the row renders with `.strike` + an "Archived" text chip, and Edit/Archive are absent while Restore is present; clicking Restore issues PATCH `{status:'active'}` with `If-Match: <version>`.
- FE api unit: `archive(id, token, bookId)` hits `DELETE /motifs/{id}?book_id=…` and `patch(..., bookId)` hits `PATCH /motifs/{id}?book_id=…` (regression guard for gap #4).
- BE: no new test needed — `archive`/`archive_shared` + the status filter are already covered in composition-service tests; if a shared-tier archive assertion is missing, add it to the existing motif repo integration test rather than a new file.

*Evidence:* services/composition-service/app/routers/motif.py:361-380 (DELETE = soft archive, `?book_id=` shared path, "NOT a hard delete — the motif_application FK is SET NULL so the binding-ledger history survives"); services/composition-service/app/db/repositories/motif_repo.py:441-460 (`UPDATE motif SET status='archived'`, owner-keyed + book_shared-keyed); services/composition-service/app/db/migrate.py:869-884 (motif_application DDL — NO status column, motif_id FK ON DELETE SET NULL); services/composition-service/app/db/models.py:832 (`MotifPatchArgs.status` ⇒ Restore = PATCH status='active'); services/composition-service/app/routers/motif.py:158,226 (`pattern="^(draft|active|archived)$"`); frontend/src/features/composition/motif/hooks/useMotifLibrary.ts:93-100 (draftsQuery — the pattern archivedQuery copies); frontend/src/features/composition/motif/api.ts:67-77 (patch/archive drop book_id → shared-tier silent no-op)

### Q-33-LIVE-BROWSER-SMOKE
CONFIRMED MANDATORY — and the code exposes one blind spot that would have made the "agent half" un-runnable at 3am, so here is the exact, buildable recipe. Do NOT weaken DoD row 5; do NOT re-litigate it (it restates the repo law `agent-gui-loop-needs-live-browser-smoke-not-raw-stream` + `frontend-5174-is-baked-prod-nginx-not-vite`).

That is exactly why frontend-tools-liveness.spec.ts:157 explicitly punts on `ui_open_studio_panel`. So the existing injection helper does NOT work inside the studio as-is, and depending on a local model *choosing* to emit the tool is non-deterministic (the spec's own S06 note). Fix: force the documented in-process fallback branch.

BUILD THIS (one new spec + one helper export, per wave/milestone that adds panels):

1. `frontend/tests/e2e/helpers/frontendToolInject.ts` — add:

### Q-33-TENANCY-READONLY
CONFIRM the spec's answer — Edit/Archive are ABSENT (conditional render), never disabled-with-a-tooltip — and FIX the redaction/tier collision that currently makes the gate lie. The policy half is already shipped correctly (MotifDetailDrawer.tsx:63 conditionally renders Edit; MotifCard.test.tsx:32 asserts the system case). The gate itself is BROKEN, and 3a must fix it. Five concrete changes:

(1) BE — stop making the FE derive tenancy from a field the server nulls. In services/composition-service/app/routers/motif.py, inside `_redact_for_viewer` (line 98), BEFORE `data["owner_user_id"] = None` (line 110), add two server-computed wire fields:
    data["tier"] = "system" if motif.owner_user_id is None else ("user" if is_owner else "public")
    data["can_edit"] = is_owner
and in `_book_view` (line 207), after the redaction call, OVERRIDE for the shared tier:
    if motif.book_shared: data["can_edit"] = True   # the caller already passed _gate_book(VIEW); EDIT is re-gated on PATCH
Apply to GET /motifs/{id}, the list projection, and /motifs/book/{book_id}. `owner_user_id` STAYS redacted — `tier` is a 3-value enum that leaks nothing about WHO owns a row, only that it isn't you, so §4.2's author-privacy property is preserved.

(2) FE — frontend/src/features/composition/motif/simpleMode.ts: `motifTier()` returns the wire `tier` when present, falling back to the owner_user_id heuristic only when absent; `isReadOnly(motif, me)` becomes `motif.can_edit === false ? true : motifTier(...) !== 'user'` (wire wins). Add `tier?: MotifTier` and `can_edit?: boolean` to `Motif` in types.ts.

(3) FE — DELETE the `CATALOG_OWNER_SENTINEL = '__catalog__'` hack (useMotifLibrary.ts:31); `catalogToMotif` stamps `tier: 'public', can_edit: false` instead.

(4) FE — MotifCard.tsx:56-58 tier chip is word+hue only. Add the GLYPH so it is glyph+word+hue per §5.3: system `🔒` · user `✎` · public `🌐` (aria-hidden on the glyph; the word carries the meaning). Keep TIER_CLASS hues.

(5) FE — 3a ADDS the Archive button (useMotifDetail.ts:31's `archive` mutation is dead — no button renders it anywhere, yet 3a's DoD demands archive work in a live browser). It MUST be `{!readOnly && <button data-testid="motif-detail-archive">}` — conditional render, never `disabled`. Also fix the stale header comment at MotifDetailDrawer.tsx:4 ("every edit control is disabled") — the code is right, the comment is wrong and would walk the porter straight into the disabled variant this row forbids.

TESTS (add to 3a DoD, all red-first):
 - simpleMode.test.ts: `{owner_user_id: null, tier: 'public'}` → tier 'public' (wire beats the null-owner heuristic); `{owner_user_id: null, can_edit: true}` → isReadOnly false.
 - MotifDetailDrawer test (NEW): readOnly=true → `queryByTestId('motif-detail-edit')` is null AND `queryByTestId('motif-detail-archive')` is null. Assert NULL, not `toBeDisabled()` — a `toBeDisabled()` assertion here is itself the bug.
 - MotifDetailDrawer test (NEW — the regression this row exists for): a `book_shared` row with `owner_user_id: null, can_edit: true` → Edit button PRESENT.
 - MotifCard.test.tsx:32: assert the chip textContent contains BOTH the glyph and the i18n word.
 - BE test_motif_router: GET another user's public motif → `tier == 'public'` AND `owner_user_id is None` (redaction still holds — no author leak).

NOT a CRITICAL stop: this is a false-NEGATIVE gate (a legitimate editor is locked out of a button), not cross-user exposure — no data leaks. Build it in 3a, don't escalate.

### Q-33-3C-DELETIONS
DELETE all three — but do NOT mirror the run. The spec's "mirror arcConformanceRunPropose for the run" is WRONG per the code and would ship a paid-action defect.

(A) conformanceRunEstimate + conformanceRunConfirm (api.ts:223-235) — DELETE, NO MIRROR. motif_conformance_run.py:74-79 raises a terminal ValueError for any scope != 'arc' ("chapter conformance is the synchronous GET trace"). A chapter-scope propose->confirm passes the LEDGER CLAIM + enqueue in actions.py:714 `_execute_conformance_run`, then the worker terminally fails => the user is charged and watches a spinner forever. That is the PO's named CRITICAL class. Chapter conformance is already served FREE by the synchronous GET (motifApi.conformance, api.ts:204 -> routers/conformance.py). So:
  1. api.ts: delete `conformanceRunEstimate` + `conformanceRunConfirm` (and `_resolveActionJob` if it has no other caller).
  2. useConformanceTrace.ts: delete `estimate` state, `mintRun`, `confirmRun`, `cancelRun`. Keep `refetch`.
  3. ConformanceTraceView.tsx: keep the `data-testid="conformance-rerun"` button but point onClick at `trace.refetch()`; DELETE the `{trace.estimate && <CostConfirmCard .../>}` block (lines ~50-59). Keep CostConfirmCard itself — ArcConformancePanel still uses it. New i18n `motif.conf.rerunFree` = "Re-read the latest conformance trace (free)" as the button title.
  4. Test: __tests__/ConformanceTraceView.test.tsx asserts a click fires exactly ONE GET .../conformance?scope=chapter and ZERO POSTs to /actions/**.
  Counterfactual for PO veto: if a chapter-scope LLM re-run is genuinely wanted, that is unbuilt ENGINE work (the docstring tracks it as D-MOTIF-CONFORMANCE-ENGINE-WIRING), not a FE slice -> defer row, not a mirror.

(B) regenerateToBeat (api.ts:300-304) + useMotifBinding.regenerateScene (useMotifBinding.ts:64-68) — REPOINT at the existing generate route exactly as the spec says. Verified: POST /v1/composition/works/{project_id}/generate exists (engine.py:326) with GenerateBody (engine.py:91-114): required `outline_node_id`, `model_source: Literal['user_model','platform_model']`, `model_ref: UUID`; `operation` defaults 'draft_scene'; `mode: 'cowrite'|'auto'` — mode='auto' returns a JSONResponse job (not a stream).
  1. api.ts: replace BOTH with one helper `regenerateScene(projectId, sceneNodeId, modelRef, modelSource, token)` -> POST `${BASE}/works/${projectId}/generate`, body `{outline_node_id: sceneNodeId, model_ref: modelRef, model_source: modelSource, operation: 'draft_scene', mode: 'auto'}`, returning `{job_id}`.
  2. model_ref/model_source have NO server defaults, so thread them: add `modelRef`/`modelSource` props to ConformanceTraceView and pass `effectiveModelRef` + "user_model" at CompositionPanel.tsx:886 (the exact values already passed to PlannerView at CompositionPanel.tsx:741). useConformanceTrace + useMotifBinding take them and call the new helper.
  3. No silent no-op (Frontend-Tool-Contract): DISABLE the per-row Regenerate button when `!modelRef`, with title "Pick a model first".

(C) FIX-NOW adjacent bug found while reading (one line, cheaper than a defer row): api.ts:257 sends `arc_template_id`, but `_ConformanceRunArgs` (mcp/server.py:3105-3117) is `ForbidExtra` (extra="forbid") and the field is **`arc_id`** — a structure_node id, NOT a template id. So the arc propose the spec told us to mirror is ITSELF 422-ing today. Rename the FE key to `arc_id`, and check that ArcTemplateLibraryView.tsx:39 (`arcTemplateId={openArc.id}`, an `ArcTemplate`) actually hands over a structure_node id; if it is a template id, thread the applied structure_node id instead (worker reads it via StructureRepo, motif_conformance_run.py:86-88). If that id is genuinely not reachable in that view, file D-ARC-CONFORM-ARCID (gate 2: structural) and keep going.

  - Click Re-run => exactly one `GET /v1/composition/works/{pid}/conformance?scope=chapter&chapter_id=…` 200; ZERO requests to `/actions/conformance_run/*`.
